et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	and under the eye is tender and moist, so that the hairs of the eyelids have fallen out, and the eyelids are heated and chafed by the burning of the tears, then this treatment is necessary.
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front;	And the ancients called it "cure by contusion", and it is that you shave the hair from the forehead of the patient who has this disease, then make three incisions in the forehead equally along the length of the forehead;
et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres;	and let one of the incisions be about two fingers wide in the middle of the forehead, going down to the nose, and the other two on the sides above the eyelids, and beware of cutting the arteries that are on both sides above the eyelids;
et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins;	and keep your hand away from the connection of the two jawbones, and let each wound be the width of three fingers joined together across;
et aies apparillie une piece d’esponge et mout de drapelz ses por essuer lou sanc, puis boute le spatumile agut de II pars de coi ci est li forme:	and have ready a piece of sponge and plenty of cloths to wipe the blood, then apply the sharp spatula on both sides of which this is the form:
des l’incision qui est dever la temple jusc’a la seconde incision;	from the incision which is towards the temple to the second incision;
et escorche tout le keur qui est entre les II fendures a tot lou syfac qui est sus l’os, puis fai autreteil des la moiene incision jusc’a l’autre seconde, et puis estrai fuer cest spatumile.	and scrape all the flesh that is between the two incisions, along with the pericranium which is on the bone, then do the same from the middle incision to the other second one, and then remove this spatula.
si boute en la premiere fendure l’estrument qui est apelez «cultellaire», et est tresbien trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part est souef, ne mie trenchans, et c’est li forme:	then put in the first incision the instrument which is called "cultellaire", which is very sharp on one side, and on the other side is smooth, not sharp, and this is its shape:
Et met le costeit taillant vers la char aerse au keur, et lou costeit souef vers l’os, et lou boute tant qu’il veigne a la moiene fendure.	And put the cutting side toward the flesh close to the heart, and the smooth side towards the bone, and insert it until it reaches the middle incision.
Et cope toz les vasselz que dessendent dou chief as eulz tant que l’incision soit continue jusc’a ceu qui apert dou keur, et puis autreteil fai en la moiene fendure jusc’a l’autre defuer;	And cut all the vessels that descend from the head to the eyes until the incision is continuous to that which opens to the heart, and then do the same in the middle incision up to the other outside [incision];
et puis estrai dou sanc igalment, et espresse lou leu por le sanc pris;	and then draw blood evenly, and compress the area because of the blood taken;
puis met en chescune fendure une tente de viel coton, et met sus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile et en aisil, et garde que apostemes chaus n’i veigne;	then put in each incision a tent of old cotton, and put on cloths soaked in wine and oil and vinegar, and watch that no hot abscesses develop;
et au tier jor deslie lou liien, et i amenistre grant planteit d’aigue tede, puis lou cure d’oignement basilicon avec oile roset, et d’autres cures dont on cure plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and on the third day untie the bandage, and apply a large amount of warm water, then treat it with basilicon ointment with rose oil, and other treatments with which one treats wounds, until it is healed.
dou reume des eulz	of eye rheum
Quant a aucun vienent catarre agut acostumeement, et tu vois les eulz tenves et petis, et afoiblir la veue, et les papieres brulees;	When someone experiences acute, recurring catarrh, and you see their eyes dim and small, and their vision weakening, and their eyelids burned;
et li poil chieent, et ou chief en parfont a dolor ague, et li malaides esternue;	and the hair falls out, and there is a sharp pain deep in the head, and the patient sneezes;
adonques saiches par ces accidens que celles matieres et cil catharre ne vient fuer que de maintes voines, et li muedre cure que i est, si est ceste.	then know by these symptoms that these matters and this catarrh come from many veins, and the best treatment there is, is this one.
Et est que tu comande au malaide a rere son front, puis fai une grant fendure emmi lou front, et une autre dou large I poc.	And it is that you instruct the patient to shave their forehead, then make a large incision in the middle of the forehead, and another one the width of a thumb.
Et comence des la fendure de la temple senestre a la temple destre, et soit li incision jusc’a l’os;	And begin from the incision at the left temple to the right temple, and let the incision go down to the bone;
et esloigne ta main des ners des temples que muevent au mengier;	and keep your hand away from the nerves of the temples that move during eating;
et quant li os est descovers, si essue tout le sanc a une esponge, et puis desevre entre les II levres de la fendure et i met coton viel, et tentes de lin;	and when the bone is exposed, wipe all the blood with a sponge, and then separate between the two edges of the incision and put in old cotton and linen tents;
puis lie desus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile, et te garde d’aposteme chaut;	then tie over it cloths soaked in wine and oil, and beware of a hot abscess;
quant il est ostez, si covient que tu frottes l’os tant que chars i comence a naistre, puis le cure de choses exiccatives, que font enjanrer char.	when it is removed, you must rub the bone until flesh begins to grow there, then treat it with drying agents, which promote the growth of flesh.
En teil maniere:	In this manner:
pren II parties de flor de froment, et de colofoine IIII parties, et en fai emplaustre;	take two parts wheat flour, and four parts colophony, and make a plaster;
et l’aministre en ces plaies por enjanrer char per tout.	and apply it to these wounds to generate flesh everywhere.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	On the blocking of the ears
Tout ceu que chiet ens oreilles est une des IIII choses:	Everything that falls into the ears is one of four things:
ou grains, ou beste, ou piere de mine ou semblans chose si com fer;	either grain, or an insect, or a mineral stone or similar thing such as iron;
ou semence, si com jaisses, feves, pois;	or a seed, such as vetch, beans, peas;
ou chose defluans si com aigue et aisilz et semblans choses.	or a flowing thing such as water and vinegar and similar things.
Quant il chiet en l’oreille piere ou autre maniere de chose que ne s’ajoste mie a l’oreille, ne ne croist en l’oreille, si met l’oreille au solel.	When a stone or other type of thing falls into the ear that does not stick to the ear, nor grows in the ear, place the ear in the sun.
Se tu vois la piere, si distille aucun poc d’oile violet ou oile de sisament, puis i amenistre extraction;	If you see the stone, then instill a little violet oil or sesame oil, then attempt extraction;
et lou fai esternuer de condisi, et li estoupe les narines quant li esternuemens vient, et met entor l’oreille pieces de drapelz ou laine;	and make him sneeze with condiments, and block his nostrils when the sneeze comes, and wrap pieces of cloth or wool around his ear;
et estent l’oreille au desus.	and stretch the ear upwards.
Mout de fois vient fuer par ceste cure;	Often it will come out with this treatment;
et s’elle ne vient fuer, se li amenistre extraction as pinceures subtilz, de coi ci est li forme:	and if it does not come out, attempt extraction with fine forceps, of which this is the form:
S’elle saut fuer as pinceures, c’est boin;	If it jumps out with the forceps, that's good;
se ceu non, si amenistre extraction a l’oncine subtil de petite doubleure;	If not, then attempt extraction with a fine hook, slightly curved;
et s’elle ne saut par ceu, si fai une caine d’arain et boute lou chief de la cainne ou pertuis de l’oreille fort, et estoupe ceu qui est entor la cainne de cire mole si que li vens n’i puisse entrer avec la cainne;	and if it doesn't jump out with that, then make a tube of bronze and push the end of the tube into the opening of the ear firmly, and plug what is around the tube with soft wax so that air cannot enter with the tube;
puis le trai fuer forment, car mout de fois vient fuer si com nos avons dit;	then pull it out strongly, because it often comes out as we have said;
et s’elle ne vient fuer en teil maniere, si prent glut de coi en prent les oisiaus, et met en som aucun estrument qui soit a point por ceu faire, et met un poc de coton entor;	And if it doesn't come out in this manner, then take birdlime, which is used to catch birds, and put some on the tip of an instrument suitable for this purpose, and put a bit of cotton around it;
puis presse le glut sus la piere ou quel chose que ce soit, et trai fuer.	then press the birdlime onto the stone or whatever it may be, and pull it out.
Et s’elle ne saut fuer de toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si te haste de fendre l’oreille ainsois que aposteme chalz i veigne, et spasme;	And if it does not come out with all these things that we have said, then hurry to cut open the ear before a hot abscess and spasm develop;
et li maniere de la fendure si est que tu faices premier sainier lou malaide de la cephalique, et estrai dou sanc selonc la mesure de sa vertu, puis fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains et li torne l’oreille au desus, et fent une petite fendure en la racine de l’oreille a la graisse ou leu dependant;	And the way to make the incision is that you first have the patient bleed from the cephalic vein, and draw blood according to their strength, then have the patient sit between your hands and turn the ear upwards, and make a small incision at the base of the ear in the fatty or adjacent area;
et soit li fendure ausi com une lune, tant que tu viegnes a la piere, puis l’oste selonc ton pooir, et la suce hastanment a ta bouche;	and the incision should be crescent-shaped, until you reach the stone, then remove it according to your ability, and quickly suck it out with your mouth;
et la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat it until it is healed.
Et se c’est grains qui est ens et il enfle, si aministre extraction;	And if it is a grain that is inside and it swells, then administer extraction;
et si’il ne puet issir, si amenistre I spatumile tenve subtil selonc ceste forme:	and if it cannot come out, then administer a thin, subtle spatula according to this form:
et amenistre incision de celui grain.	and administer an incision of that grain.
Mais ne faire mie ceu quant tu penses que li grains est moistes por la moistor de l’oreille, tant que tu en aies fait maintes pieces;	But do not do this when you think the grain is moist because of the moisture of the ear, until you have made many pieces of it;
puis l’estrai as pinceures subtilz et au succier, si com nos avons dit, si que li estractions soit aligie.	then extract it with fine forceps and by suction, as we have said, so that the extraction is alleviated.
En l’aigue donques que chiet en l’oreille covient que li malaides use d’esternuement de condisi premiers, et ample l’oreille de viel coton.	For water that falls into the ear, the patient must first use sneezing powders, and fill the ear with old cotton.
Et soit gisans sus celle oreille meisme ou li aigue est.	And lie on the same ear where the water is.
s’elle saut fuer per ceu, c’est boin.	If it comes out because of this, that is good. 
se ceu non, si prent maintes pieres selonc li longesce de ton doit tenves et legieres, et les eschaufe un poc au feu;	If not, take many stones the length of your little finger, thin and light, and heat them a little in the fire;
et em mette li malaides une ou pertus de son oreille, et saille sus i. de ses piez d’autre part, et fiere d’une autre piere sus la piere qui est en l’oreille;	and the patient puts one in the opening of his ear, and jumps up and down on one foot, and strikes the stone that is in the ear with another stone; 
et ne cesse de faire ceu de piere em piere tant que li aigue isse toute fuer, et ensi saut elle toute fuer;	and do not stop doing this from stone to stone until all the water comes out, and thus it will all come out; 
et se tu vues, si prent I jonc, et boute l’un des chiés en l’oreille, et l’autre chief emprent de feu tant que li plus dou jonc soit ars;	and if you wish, take a rush, and put one end in the ear, and light the other end until most of the rush is burned;
puis refai autreteil d’autres jons tant que li aigue isse toute, si com nos avons dit en la piere.	then do the same with other rushes until all the water comes out, as we have said with the stone.
En l’estraction de la beste, s’elle est de petit cors, si com puce et semblans chose, cure la si com nos avons dit en la division;	In extracting the creature, if it is small-bodied, like a flea and similar things, treat it as we have said in the section;
mais s’elle est de grant cors c’on la puisse sentir, si amenistre extraction de pinceures;	but if it is large-bodied so that it can be felt, then administer extraction with forceps;
et c’est li chose plus legiere a oster qui soit en l’oreille.	and this is the easiest thing to remove that is in the ear.
En l’estraction des vers enjanrez as oreilles, quant tu lou cures si com nos avons dit en la division et ou traitier des distillations, et li cure ne profite mie, si covient que tu regardes l’oreille au soleil:	In the extraction of worms generated in the ears, when you treat them as we have said in the section on and in the treatment of distillations, and the treatment is not effective, then you must examine the ear in the sunlight:
s’il i apert nulz vers, si les trai as pinceures subtilz, et s’il n’aperent, si prent la cainne de coi ci est li forme:	if any worms appear, pull them out with fine forceps, and if they don't appear, take the cannula which has this shape:
Et soit estroite desoz et large desus.	And let it be narrow below and wide above.
Et boute lou plus subtil chief en l’oreille selonc la quantiteit de la soffrance dou malaide, puis succe forment a tot la caine;	And put the narrowest end into the ear according to the degree of the patient's discomfort, then suck strongly with the cannula;
fai ceu sovent tant que tuit li ver issent.	do this often until all the worms come out.
Et s’il n’obeissent a issir, si estoupe entor la cainne de coton si com j’ai dit en la piere;	And if they don't come out, then pack cotton around the cannula as I described for stones;
et s’il ne saillent fuer si com nos avons dit, si aministre distillations que li ancien ont esprovees en l’ocision des vers, et tu les troveras ou traitier des distillations;	and if they don't jump out as we have said, then administer distillations that the ancients have proven effective in killing worms, and you will find them in the treatise on distillations;
et si distille tes oiles et tes medicines en l’oreille a tout cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme si com tu vois:	and distill your oils and medicines into the ear with this instrument, of which here is the form as you see:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain estrois desoz a I petis pertuis, et desus overs por distiller;	And it should be made of silver or brass, narrow below with a small hole, and open above for distilling;
et por presser dedens la distillation a I estrument d’arain bien fait por ceu, et se tu vues pren I raseur et envoloupe entor la pointe avenanment coton;	and to press the distillation inside, use a well-made brass instrument for this purpose, and if you wish, take a razor and carefully wrap cotton around the tip;
puis i giete ton oile ou ton jus, et ceu que tu vues de tes medicines en la cainne, et li caine soit en l’oreille;	then pour your oil or juice, and whatever medicine you want, into the cannula, and the cannula should be in the ear;
puis boute dedens lou raseur a tout lou coton, et presse ta main tempreement tant que li oile soit distilleit ou chevement de l’oreille;	then insert the razor with the cotton, and press your hand gently until the oil is distilled into the cavity of the ear;
et lou sente li malaides dedens, et soit li distillations I poc eschaufee au feu ainsois c’on la distille en l’oreille;	and the patient should feel it inside, and the distillation should be slightly warmed by fire before it is distilled into the ear;
et garde qu’elle ne soit trop froide, car li medicine ne seroit mie si bone.	and be careful that it is not too cold, because the medicine would not be as effective.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	On the blockage of ears
Aucun enfant naissent qui n’ont nul pertus ens oreilles;	Some children are born without any openings in their ears;
et ceste meisme chose avient as homes par estoupement de plaie, ou de char nee dedens l’oreille, et cist estoupemens vient aucune fois em parfont en l’oreille, si c’on ne lou puet veoir;	and this same thing happens to men by the blockage of a wound, or by flesh born inside the ear, and this blockage sometimes occurs deep in the ear, so that it cannot be seen;
et aucune fois avient I poc defuer lou pertus, et lou voit om bien.	and sometimes it happens that the opening is almost closed, and one sees it well.
Celle donques que vient em parfont, si c’on ne la puet veoir, est de grief sanation em plusors dispositions, et en cele c’on voit covient que tu mettes l’oreille dou malaide au soleil;	The one that occurs deep inside, so that one cannot see it, is difficult to heal in several situations, and in the one that can be seen, you must place the patient's ear in the sunlight; 
et regarde dedens:	and look inside:
se tu vois l’opilation apparent, si la oevre a tot cest spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	if you see the blockage apparent, then open it with this spatula of which the form is here:
Et soit agus et trenchans devant et derrier tout plain, si qu’il ne blece l’oreille;	And it should be sharp and cutting at the front and back, entirely flat, so that it does not injure the ear;
se li opilation est de char nee ou cors de l’oreille, si la tien as pinceures subtilz, et la cope legierement, tant que celle chars soit toute ostee.	if the blockage is from flesh born in or on the body of the ear, grasp it with fine forceps, and cut it lightly, until all that flesh is removed.
Et se li opilations est em parfont en l’oreille, si pren I raseur subtil legier et l’eschaufe un petit au feu, puis li met ou cors de l’oreille.	And if the blockage is deep within the ear, take a thin, light razor and warm it a little in the fire, then place it in the body of the ear.
Se tu sens l’opilation dont li malaides sent grieteit a l’oïr, perce legierement, et garde que tu ne grever les ners de l’oreille;	If you feel the blockage which causes the patient difficulty hearing, pierce it lightly, and be careful not to damage the nerves of the ear; 
puis met en l’oreille une tente selonc la largesce dou pertus, et la moille en l’oignement egyptien.	then place in the ear a tent according to the width of the opening, and soak it in Egyptian ointment.
Fai ceu aucun jor tant que li plaie soit soudee, ou tu pren une tente et la moille en aigue rose, et poudre sus vitriole broiet;	Do this for several days until the wound is healed, or take a tent and soak it in rose water, and powder it with crushed vitriol;
et se tu vois enflee l’oreille, si couvient que tu traies la tente et remue une autre tente moillie en cerote qui soit fait d’oile roset et de cire, tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	and if you see the ear swell, you must remove the tent and replace it with another tent soaked in cerate which is made of rose oil and wax, until the swelling is gone;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si plonge une esponge et drapelz en aigue froide, et le met sus l’oreille, et use d’autres cures qui oste lou decorrement de sanc qui sont ou traitier des destillations.	And if bleeding occurs, soak a sponge and cloths in cold water and place them on the ear, and use other treatments that stop the bleeding which are in the treatise on distillations.
de la char des papieres	of the flesh of papyrus
Cist althelul que vienent em papieres des eulz quant ils sont moiste et sont sec, si covient que tu les estendes de tenailles et de pinceures, et le cope d’un spatumile de ses racines;	These little growths that appear on the eyelids when they are moist and dry must be pulled out with forceps and tweezers, and the root cut with a small spatula; 
puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet.	then apply ground vitriol to the area.
Et se sans en decort, si le cauterize dou cautere lenticulaire subtil, et li cauterizeir aprés l’incision vaut mues;	And if blood flows, cauterize it with a fine lenticular cautery, and cauterizing after the incision is worth a lot;
et maintes fois repairent, cant aucune chose demoure de lor racines;	and they often return, when some of their roots remain;
et quant elles sont cauterizees par feu, si sont arses celles racines et ne revienent mie.	and when they are cauterized with fire, those roots are burned and they do not return.
de la gresle	of hail
Maintes fois vienent em papieres des eulz unes choses que semblent gresle en sa forme et en sa duresce, et por ceu est ceste maladie apelee «grandine», et est une assemblee de moistor grosse en la papiere desus et desoz;	Often there appear in the eyelids things that resemble hail in their form and hardness, and for this reason this disease is called "hailstone", and it is a collection of thick moisture in the eyelid above and below;
li ovraiges est telz:	the procedure is as follows:
pren warde se li grandine se muet d’une part et d’autre, et c’est legiere chose a savoir;	observe if the hailstone moves from one side to the other, and this is easy to determine;
fent la donques dou large, puis l’escorche de chescune partie legierement, puis la prent as pinceures, et la cope.	then make a wide incision, then peel it gently from each side, then grasp it with tweezers, and cut it out.
se tu ne la pues coper sens percier un poc la papiere, si ne grieve rien au malaide;	if you cannot cut it out without piercing the eyelid a little, it does not harm the patient;
et se li fendure est grans, si l’assemble a une costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	and if the tear is large, join it with a suture, and treat it until it is healed;
et s’elle est petite, si n’i faire point de force, car li oignemens la restoure tantost et enjanre char.	and if it is small, do not exert any force, for the ointment will soon restore it and generate flesh.
Et se li grandine est dessendans au dedens de l’oreille vers la partie desus, si enverse la papiere, et estent la grandine a unes pinceures, et la cope et presse d’une part et d’autre;	And if the hailstone is descending inside the ear toward the upper part, invert the eyelid, and grasp the hailstone with tweezers, and cut it out and press from both sides;
et se li papiere est esloignie par l’incision, ce ne grieve rien;	and if the eyelid is separated by the incision, it does not matter;
et quant li grandine est copee, si leive l’oil d’aigue salee, et cure le leu de ceu qui enjanre char tant que li malaides soit sanez.	and when the hailstone is removed, wash the eye with salt water, and treat the area with something that generates flesh until the patient is healed.
de la graisse des eulz	of the fat of the eyes
Exinach est une graisse qui est enjanree en toiles des papieres desus, et ce avient plus as enfans c’a nules gens, et grieve mout a lor eulz, et li vienent li catharre as matinees, et ne pueent regardeir la lumiere dou soleil por ceu que les larmes se hastent a lor eulz;	Exinach is a fat that is generated in the tissues of the upper eyelids, and this happens more to children than to any other people, and it greatly bothers their eyes, and they have mucus in the mornings, and they cannot look at the sunlight because tears rush to their eyes;
et por ceu se couchent il sor lor faices adés, et dorment sus, et sont lor papieres desoz lor sorcilz moistes que li enfleure et li apparance ont covert de l’exinach qui apert en l’oil.	and because of this they constantly lie on their faces, and sleep on them, and their eyelids below their eyebrows are moist, which swelling and appearance are covered by the exinach that is visible in the eye.
Et quant tu presses lou leu a tes dois et sent l’exirnach entr’ous.	And when you press the area with your fingers and feel the exinach between them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain;	And the method of the procedure is that the patient puts their head in your lap;
et puis pren I drapeil de lin, et appareille une tente em maniere d’un cercle selonc la quantiteit que conteigne exirnach de chescune partie, puis le met sus li;	and then take a linen cloth, and prepare a tent in the shape of a circle according to the amount of exinach contained on each side, then put it on them;
et presse a tes dois d’une part et d’autre, si que li exirnach soit assemblez emmi le cercle;	and press with your fingers on one side and the other, so that the exinach is gathered in the middle of the circle;
puis fent em mileu de la moistor au spatumile trenchant une fendure dou large, et ne soit mie plus grans que li plaie c’on fait a la sainie de voinne;	then split the moisture in the middle with a sharp spatula, making a cut the width of, and no larger than, the incision made for bloodletting;
et fent le cuir em parfont tant que tu veignes a l’exirnach;	and cut the skin deeply until you reach the exinach;
et em plusors dispositions vient exirnach de la fendure, selonc la forme d’une piece de graisse blainche.	and in several instances, exinach comes out of the cut, looking like a piece of white fat.
Estrai la donques a tout une piece de drap charpit entre tes dois au defuer, et torne ta main a destre et a senestre tant qu’il soit espars;	Then extract it all in one piece with a cloth grasped between your fingers over the fire, and turn your hand right and left until it is removed;
et garde que tu n’ajoster en la fendure, que tu ne viegnes a tout le spatumile jusc’a l’oil, que tu ne le bleces.	and be careful not to push into the cut, that you do not reach all the way to the eye with the spatula, lest you injure it.
Et se li exirnach n’apert en l’encomencement de la fendure, si acroi un poc la fendure legierement tant qu’il apere;	And if the exinach does not appear at the beginning of the incision, then enlarge the incision slightly until it appears;
puis l’estrai si com nos avons dit, puis moille drapelz en aisil et en aigue, et met sus le leu, et estrain de bendelz.	then extract it as we have said, then soak cloths in vinegar and water, and place them on the area, and bind with bandages.
Et si a de tels homes qui broient seil et mettent sus por corrompre cele moistor qui est demoree.	And there are some men who grind salt and apply it to break down the remaining moisture.
Puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat it until it is healed.
Et s’il vient au leu aposteme chaut, si lou cure d’emplaustres assouajant tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if a hot abscess develops at the site, treat it with soothing plasters until it is healed.
des poilz des papieres	of the hairs of the eyelids
Quant em papieres naissent poilz ajostez autre que li naturez, et sont enveillit, si nuisent as eulz, et font venir manieres de maladies si com larmes acostumees et mollifications des papieres et albugine, tant que c’est cause de la destruction des eulz;	When hairs grow on the eyelids in addition to the natural ones, and become irritating, they harm the eyes and cause various ailments such as habitual tears and softening of the eyelids and albugo, to the point of causing the destruction of the eyes;
et est li cure selonc IIII manieres:	and the treatment is according to four methods:
ou par cautere ensamble feu, ou par medicine ague selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre de cautere, et est fais ou par incision et costure ou par caines, selonc ceu que je dirai.	either by cautery with fire, or by sharp medicine according to what is described above in the chapter on cautery, and it is done either by incision and stitching or by small tubes/pipes, as I will explain.
Il covient que tu mettes lou chief dou malaide en ton sain, puis torne la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre;	You should place the patient's head in your lap, then turn back the eyelid with your left hand;
s’elle est convertie, c’est boin;	if it is inverted/turned outwards, it is good;
se ceu non, si i boute une aguille a tout I fil desus;	if not, then insert a needle with a thread through it;
et soit ce delez la marge de la papiere ou li poil naissent delez ces poilz, et trai I fil au desus a tout la papiere, et la torne au raseur;	and let this be near the edge of the eyelid where the eyelashes grow, near these hairs, and pull the thread up along with the eyelid, and turn it towards the surgeon/barber;
puis fent en la partie desoz la papiere, desoz les poilz ajostez, a tout le spatumile copant, des le grant larmier jusc’au petit;	then cut in the part below the eyelid, beneath the eyelashes, with the spatula-shaped knife, from the large tear duct to the small one;
puis estrai I fil, et met desoz la papiere une petite tente de couton et de drapeil, puis seigne sus la papiere une figure d’enche, si com la fuelle de mirte, et toutevoie il covient que li figure soit selonc la quantiteit que tu vues eslever la papiere qui est devisez a toz.	then remove the thread, and place under the eyelid a small tent of cotton and cloth, then draw on the eyelid a figure with ink, like a myrtle leaf, and however, it must be that the figure is according to the amount that you want to raise the eyelid which is separated from the others.
Et si a teil qui a mestier c’on cope grant quantiteit de la papiere selonc ceu que li papiere est mollifie;	And there are some who need a large amount of the eyelid cut, depending on how softened the eyelid is;
puis fent a tout le spatumile sus les II lignes que tu as signiet, et comence des lou grant larmier jusc’a petit;	then cut with the spatula-shaped knife along the two lines that you have marked, and begin from the large tear duct to the small one;
et soit li une des fendures pres des poilz naturez en la groissece d’un raiz, puis boute l’oncine en l’un des II angles dou keur, puis l’escorche toute;	and let one of the cuts be near the natural eyelashes about the thickness of a hair, then place the hook in one of the two angles of the heart shape, then peel it all off;
puis assemble les II levres a une costure d’une aguille a tout I fil de laine subtil, et essue le sanc, et fai aerdre la superfluiteit des filz sus les II sorcilz a tout aucunes choses gluans, se tu vues faire ce;	then join the two edges with a suture using a needle and a thin woolen thread, and wipe the blood, and burn the excess threads above the eyebrows with some sticky substance, if you wish to do so;
et se ce non, si n’en aies cure, puis laisse la costure et les filz jusc’a III jors ou IIII;	and if not, don't worry about it, then leave the suture and the threads for three or four days;
puis cure la plaie sens costure de choses sechans et constrignans, car li papiere se relive au soudement de la plaie et l’assemblement de li, mais li costure est muedre (si com dirent li ancien), et c’est ovraiges sens paor;	then treat the wound without stitching, with drying and constricting substances, for the eyelid lifts itself up when the wound closes and joins together, but stitching is better (as the ancients said), and this is a painless procedure;
et si a une autre maniere:	and there is another method:
et est que tu seignes la papiere d’une figure qui soit ausi com li fuelle de mirte, si com nos avons conteit, a III oncines desevrez selonc la forme qui est ci:	and that is you mark the eyelid with a figure shaped like a myrtle leaf, as we have described, with three points separated according to the shape shown here:
puis cope ceu qui sormonte as petites forces igalment selonc la forme qui est ci:	then cut what is protruding with small, even cuts according to the shape shown here:
Et se tu n’as pooir de tenir les tenailles, et li chose n’est mie igalz, si prent une aguille ou il ait I fil, et la boute emmi la figure;	And if you are unable to hold the forceps, and the thing is not even, then take a needle with a thread in it, and place it in the middle of the figure;
et boute I autre fil delez lou grant larmier, et lou secont fil delez lou petit, et assemble entre tes dois les filz igalment;	and place another thread next to the large tear duct, and the second thread next to the small one, and gather the threads evenly between your fingers;
puis lieve ta main igalment, et lieve tout le cuir sus coi tu as signiet, si com nos avons conteit, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie par costure, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	then lift your hand evenly, and lift all the skin on which you have made the mark, as we have described, then bring together the two edges of the wound by stitching, and treat it until it is healed; 
et se aposteme vient a ton incision, si l’apaise de cerote et de semblans oignement assouajans;	and if an abscess develops at your incision, soothe it with a plaster and similar soothing ointments;
et aucune fois avient que li poil de la papiere sont convertit:	and sometimes it happens that the hairs of the eyelid are turned inwards:
si covient que tu uses ceu que nos avons dit de l’incision;	so you must use what we have said about the incision;
mais li costure en l’une et en l’autre est plus artificialz.	but the stitching in one and the other is more specialized.
Li cure des caines si est selonc ceste forme:	The treatment of dog bites is as follows:
et est que tu convertisses la papiere et la fent dedens selonc ceu que j’ai dit, et puis fai II caines par art, et II liiens subtilz ausi lonc com li papiere et li largesce dou spatumile est;	and it is that you turn the eyelid and slit it inside as I have said, and then make two incisions skillfully, and two fine threads as long as the eyelid and the width of the spatula;
et cope as II chiés de II pars ou tu tiens les filz;	and cut at the two ends on the two sides where you hold the threads;
puis assemble l’un et l’autre subtilment sus ceu que sormonte de la papiere de l’oil, et estrain les II cainnes des II parties forment;	then join one and the other delicately over what protrudes from the eyelid, and tighten the two incisions of the two parts firmly;
et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, et li cuir qui iert estrainte morra et nercira et porrira, tant qu’il cherra par lui.	and leave it thus for some days, and the skin that was constricted will die and blacken and rot, until it falls off by itself.
S’il tarde, si le cope a unes forces, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	If it delays, then cut it with scissors, then treat it until it is healed;
et quant li plaie iert soudee, et si ert levee li papiere, et ne poindront plus li poil;	and when the wound is closed, the eyelid will be lifted, and the hairs will no longer prick;
et c’est li forme des II cainnes que tu feras selonc ceste figure, et selonc ceste quantiteit de lonc et de large:	and this is the shape of the two incisions that you will make according to this figure, and according to this quantity of length and width:
li ovraiges est telz que tu preignes une aguille subtil, et i boute I fil de soie souef et subtil;	The procedure is such that you take a fine needle, and thread a soft and fine silk thread through it;
puis assemble les chiés et noe l’un et l’autre subtilment, et soit li longesce des filz une palme de lonc;	then bring the ends together and knot them both subtly, and the length of the threads should be one palm long;
puis ordene en la chasse I autre fil subtil de soie briément, et noe les chief dou fil;	then arrange in the instrument another short, fine silk thread, and knot the ends of the thread;
puis mette li malaides son chief en ton sain;	then have the patient put their head in your lap;
et soit delez lou soleil si que li ovraiges soit declairiez, car c’est uns ovraiges subtilz et menus, puis boute l’aguille a tout la chasse en la racine dou poil ajosteit, et la fai percier en la papiere hastanment tant que tu la traies desus lou poil natureil;	and be near the sun so that the work is illuminated, for it is a subtle and delicate task, then insert the needle with the instrument at the root of the hair next to it, and pierce it through the caruncle quickly until you pull it out over the natural hair;
puis estrai le poil jusque sus la chasse, et boute en la chasse celui poil, s’il en i a I ou II ou III ou plusors;	then pull the hair up to the instrument, and insert that hair into the instrument, whether there is one or two or three or more;
puis estrai ta main tant que li poilz veigne fuers a tout la chasse en la papiere avec lou poil natureil.	then pull your hand so that the hair comes out with the instrument in the caruncle along with the natural hair.
Et se li chasse est traite et li poilz ne vient fuer avec li, si trairas la chasse au desoz a tout le fil que tu i as ordeneit, tant que li chasse veigne fuer dou pertus desus et que tu la voies par la vision de l’oil;	And if the instrument is pulled and the hair does not come out with it, then you will pull the instrument from below with the thread that you have arranged there, until the instrument comes out of the hole above and you see it with the vision of your eye;
adonques si trairas la chasse et le fil, et clo l’oil et lou laisse clo II jors ou III, tant que li poil s’aerde en son leu et naisse li char sus;	then you will pull the instrument and the thread, and close the eye and leave it closed for two or three days, until the hair is burned in its place and the flesh grows over it;
et se li poilz est petis, si acompaigne I poil lonc des chevoulz naturez, et soit alevez avec celui ou tu le laisse, tant qu’il soit eslongiez et puis le lieve.	and if the hair is short, add a long natural hair, and lift it with the one where you leave it, until it is lengthened and then remove it.
de la porriture de l’oil	of the rotting of the eye
Quant ceste maladie qui est apelee «aleacrati» ou li porriture vient en l’oil, si en i a de II manieres:	When this disease, which is called "alacratia" or rotting, affects the eye, there are two types:
l’une natureil, et l’autre innatureil.	one natural, and the other unnatural.
Et avient par soudement de plaie, ou de tailleure ou de cautere, et par semblans choses.	And it occurs from a sudden wound, or a cut, or a cautery, and similar things.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige en li est que tu fendes celle soudure, et dessevre les levres de li, et met dedens tentes de lin, et la lie tant qu’elle soit sanee;	And the method of treatment is that you cut open that seam/suture, and separate its lips/edges, and put linen tents inside, and bind it until it is healed;
et ne covient mie que tu uses en la cure de li de choses que sechent et restraignent.	and you must not use in its treatment things that dry and constrict.
Car se tu fais ceu, si revient li maladie pire que li premiere;	For if you do this, the illness will return worse than the first time;
mais i oevre de choses amollissans, si com fenugreic;	but treat it with softening things, such as fenugreek;
et l’arose d’aigue ou altee et semence de lin soient cuites, et oignemens dyaquilon fondut en aucun des oiles, et i envoloupe une tente, et le cure de ceu.	and bathe it with water in which marshmallow and linseed have been boiled, and ointments of melted diachylon in some oil, and wrap a tent in it, and treat it with this.
Et li tresors de ta cure si est que tu te dones en garde qu’ele ne soude mie selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant;	And the key to your treatment is to be careful that it does not heal in the same shape as it was before; 
et cist ovraiges que nos avons dit nen est fuers que adresemens de ceste maladie, qu’elle ne reviegne selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant.	and this work that we have described is nothing other than the correction of this illness, so that it does not return in the form it was before.
de la char qui vient en l’oil	of the flesh that grows in the eye
Ceste maladie que est desoz qui vraiement est apelee «axacrati», et est naturelz et accidens.	This disease, which is below, is truly called "axacrati", and is both natural and accidental. 
Li accidens vient de plaie et de fendure et de cautere et de choses semblans;	The accidental type comes from wounds and cracks and cauterization and similar things;
et li voie de l’ovraige en li si est que tu preignes un aguille, en coi il ait I fil double, et la fiche en la char, et li fai percier des le senestre larmier tant c’a destre, si que li filz veigne en II chiés de la char;	and the way to operate on it is that you take a needle, in which there is a double thread, and stick it in the flesh, and make it pierce from the left tear duct to the right, so that the thread comes out at both ends of the flesh;
puis estent la char au desus a tout l’aguille, et la cope a I spatumile large.	then stretch the flesh above with the needle, and cut it with a spatula one finger wide.
Et se li figure de la papiere revient selonc ceu qu’il covient, c’est boin;	And if the form of the eyelid returns as it should, it is good;
se ceu non, si pren I raseur et le met en la fendure, et torne la papiere, et fent II fendures ou costeit dedens la papiere;	if not, then take a razor and put it in the crack, and turn the eyelid, and make two incisions on the side inside the eyelid;
et soient li chiés des II fendures des II angles de l’incision que tu as copeit, et soit fais uns angles si que quant elles sont assemblees, que li figure soit ausi com li figure d’une lettre qui a non «I griesche»;	and let the ends of the two incisions be at the two angles of the incision that you cut, and make an angle so that when they are assembled, the shape is like the shape of a letter called "Greek I"; (or "Y")
puis oste celle char, selonc la quantiteit que ses costez est agus desoz, de ceu qui enseut la papiere, puis ajoste les II parties desevrees, et les cout d’un fil de lainne;	then remove that flesh, according to how much its sides are sharp underneath, from what is attached to the eyelid, then join the two separated parts, and sew them with a woolen thread;
puis lou cure de ceu que nos avons dit des medicines mollifians, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it with what we have said about softening medicines, and with tents, until it is healed.
Et se li maladie vient de fendure ou de costure ou de cautere, si covient que tu fendes une fendure plainne desoz les poilz des papieres, et selonc ceu qui est ci devant;	And if the illness comes from a crack or a seam or a cautery, then you must make a full incision under the hairs of the eyelids, and according to what is described above;
puis desevre entre les II leivres d’une tente, si com j’ai dit;	then separate between the two edges with a tent, as I have said;
et doit on faire l’ovraige selonc la forme de la maladie, car elle est mout diverse en forme, et li saiges maistres appareille engien de tout som pooir coment il faice revenir la figure a sa forme natureil;	and the work must be done according to the form of the illness, for it is very diverse in form, and the wise master devises with all his power how he can return the appearance to its natural form;
et li malaides meisme, selonc ceu qu’il i covient d’ovraige et d’estrumens em plusors dispositions.	and the patient himself, according to what is required in terms of work and instruments in various arrangements.
dou soudement de la papiere	of the stitching of the eyelid
Quant ceste soudure avient a mains homes en teil maniere que li papiere desus est sodee avec le blanc de l’oil, et ne puet movoir ne faire ses ovraiges naturez, si covient donques que tu i boutes la pointe d’un raseur desoz la papiere, et la lieve en haut;	When this adhesion happens to some men in such a way that the upper eyelid is attached to the white of the eye, and cannot move or perform its natural functions, then you must insert the point of a razor under the eyelid, and lift it upwards;
et l’estent as pinceures, tant que tu copes ceu qui est aert au spatumile subtil, qui ne soit mie trop agus ne trop trenchans, si que li malaides ne puisse soffrir que li spatumile trop agus ne blecent l’oil;	and stretch it with small tweezers, until you cut what is stuck with a subtle spatula, which should not be too sharp or too cutting, so that the patient can tolerate it and the too sharp spatula does not injure the eye;
et soit ton incision, dont tu escorche celle assemblee, legierement, si que li papiere reviegne selonc sa forme natureil;	and make your incision, with which you peel away this adhesion, lightly, so that the eyelid returns to its natural shape;
et est sanee toute celle assemblee, et font aucune fois en l’oil aigue salee, et le leve d’aigue douce, et de coliere;	and this entire adhesion is healed, and they sometimes put salt water in the eye, and then rinse it with fresh water, and with an eyewash;
puis met entre la papiere et l’oil une tente de lin, et met sus l’oil laine moillie en abun d’uef;	then place between the eyelid and the eye a linen tent, and place over the eye wool soaked in egg white;
et aprés le tier jor use dou coliere et des choses soudans tant qu’il soit sanez.	and after the third day, use the eyewash and desiccating remedies until it is healed.
de l’ungle de l’oil	of the nail of the eye
Saiches que li ungle est selonc II manieres:	Know that the nail (pterygium) is of two kinds:
elle est nervouse et semblans a I dur syfac, et une autre qui n’est mie nervouse, mais est semblans a blainche moistor congelee, que quant on la touche de fer et on la cuide panre as pinceures, si ne puet om;	one is fibrous and resembles a hard tumor, and the other is not fibrous, but resembles a frozen white moisture, that when one touches it with iron and tries to grasp it with forceps, one cannot;
et l’une et l’autre semblance encomence devers le grant larmier, et croist poc et poc tant qu’ele cuevre toute la veue et toute la lumiere et le movement de l’oil.	and both kinds begin near the tear duct, and grow little by little until they cover all the sight and all the light and the movement of the eye.
Et li maniere de l’incision si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz;	And the manner of the incision is that the patient puts his head on your lap, then opens his eyes;
et lieve la papiere a ta main, puis coil l’ungle as pinceures de petite doubleure, et l’estent au desus;	and lift the eyelid with your hand, then grasp the nail with the forceps, bending it slightly, and stretching it upwards;
puis pren une aguille, et i met I poil de cheval, ou de vaiche, ou de buef, et I fil fort;	then take a needle, and put in it a horsehair, or a cow hair, or an ox hair, and a strong thread;
et double la pointe de l’aguille un poc et la fiche emmi l’ungle, et la perce a tout l’aguille, et lie l’ungle d’un fil et l’estent au desus, et escorche a tout lou poil le costeit de l’ungle qui enseut la prunele et la soie au poil jusc’au chief, puis cope lou remanant en la racine dou larmier a tout lou spatumile subtil et as petites forces, et laisse la char natureil ou larmier, si que par l’incision ne veigne li cors des larmes acostumeement;	and bend the point of the needle a little and insert it in the middle of the nail, and pierce it through with the whole needle, and tie the nail with a thread and stretch it upwards, and scrape with the hair the side of the nail that follows the pupil and the white of the eye up to the top, then cut the remainder at the root of the tear duct with a very fine spatumile and with little force, and leave the natural flesh in the tear duct, so that the flow of tears does not become accustomed to the incision;
et aucune fois s’estent li ungle a l’oncine soulement, et au fil, si com nos avons dit;	and sometimes the nail is stretched with the hook only, and with the thread, as we have said;
puis l’escorche on a tout le spatumile souef de coi ci est li forme:	then it is scraped with the spatumile gently, which has this shape:
Et garde que li spatumile ne touche la toile charnue et la rompe, et que li prunele ne soit percie;	And be careful that the spatumile does not touch the fleshy tissue and tear it, and that the pupil is not pierced;
et aprés l’incision giete en l’oil un poc de seil broiet, et dou coliere fait de litargire, et le laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;	and after the incision put a little crushed salt in the eye, and some collyrium made of litharge, and leave it until the next day;
puis le cure de ceu qu’il i covient tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it with what is necessary until it is healed.
Et se li ungle n’est mie nervouse, et tu ne pues bouter l’aguille, et li uncines n’i puet entrer, maintes fois est curee ceste semblance d’ungle de medicines;	And if the nail is not sinewy, and you cannot insert the needle, and the hook cannot enter, often this type of nail is treated with medicines;
et naissent sicom j’ai conteit en la division, et se tu la vues coper, si oevre l’oil dou malaide, et pren le spatumile legier poc agut selonc ceste forme:	and they grow as I have explained in the section, and if you wish to cut it, then open the patient's eye, and take a smooth spatumile, slightly sharp, in this shape:
Et reis l’ungle desus subtilment, et se tu vois qu’elle amenuise point et li rasion i apresse, si distille de ta bouche en l’oil coliere fait de litargire et dou coliere rouge et seil broiet, et estoupe l’oil jusc’a l’autre jor;	And scrape the nail above subtly, and if you see that it diminishes somewhat and the root comes close, then instill in the eye a collyrium made of litharge and red collyrium and crushed salt from your mouth, and cover the eye until the next day;
puis rencomence l’autre ovraige selonc ceste meisme oevre, tant qu’elle soit toute ostee.	then recommence the other work according to this same method, until it is completely removed.
Se aucune chose ne t’est contraire en l’oil, si com aposteme chaus, adonques la lait, et cure premier l’aposteme chaut tant qu’il soit sanez, puis rencomence l’ovraige si com devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If something is wrong with the eye, such as a hot abscess, then leave it, and treat the hot abscess first until it is healed, then recommence the work as before, until it is healed.
Et se li apparance de la chair dou larmier nuit en l’oil par grant nuisement, si la sospent a l’oncine, et en cope une partie et non mie tot, que cors de larmes n’i viegne;	And if the appearance of the flesh of the caruncle harms the eye greatly, then lift it with a hook, and cut a part of it and not all, so that a flow of tears doesn't come;
puis distille en l’oil coliere rouge qui est fais de litargire.	then instill in the eye red collyrium which is made of litharge.
de la char qui naist sus la prunelle	of the flesh that grows on the pupil/surface of the eye
Es eulz d’aucuns homes naist aucune fois char rouge, et cuevre la prunele et restraint sus les papieres et les torne au defuer, et semble une rose de balauste;	In the eyes of some men sometimes grows red flesh, and it covers the pupil and presses on the eyelids and turns them outwards, and resembles a pomegranate blossom; 
et li ovraiges si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz, et coil toute celle char as uncines convenaubles a ceu, et la sostien a la force;	and the procedure is that the patient puts his head in your lap, then you open his eyes, and lift all this flesh with hooks suitable for this, and hold it firmly;
puis cope la premiere char, et vai tout copant au raseur jusc’a la fin, et te garde que tu ne bleces l’oil a l’ovraige;	then cut the first layer of flesh, and continue cutting with the scalpel to the end, and be careful not to injure the eye during the procedure;
et soit li incision dou spatumile que nos avons dit en l’incision de l’ungle et as petites forces de coi on oste lou sebel, si com li forme aprés cest chapistre lou demostre;	and make the incision with the spatula that we mentioned in the incision of the nail and with the small forceps with which the sebum is removed, as the figure after this chapter shows;
et quant li incision est acomplie et ostee toute li char, si emple l’oil de seil broiet ou tu i distille coliere rouge et semblans medicines corrosives, et met sus l’oil defuer coton avec abin d’uef, si qu’il soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut;	and when the incision is complete and all the flesh removed, then fill the eye with crushed salt or instill red bile and similar corrosive medicines, and put on the external eye cotton with egg white, so that it is protected from a hot abscess;
et s’il i demore rien, et li sans chaus te sormonte, et tu doutes aposteme chaut, si laisse l’oil et cure l’aposteme de choses apaisant aposteme chaut;	and if anything remains, and hot blood overcomes you, and you fear a hot abscess, then leave the eye and treat the abscess with things that soothe a hot abscess;
puis revien a ton ovraige tant qu’il soit sanez, et ensi fai cant chars est ajostee en l’oil par ceste semblance.	then return to your work until it is healed, and thus you make flesh grow back in the eye by this method.
Mais toutevoie il covient que tu aliges la cure de chescun oil foible de la voie natureil;	But nevertheless, you must lighten the treatment of each weak eye in a natural way;
et de la voie accident, en ovraige de fer;	and in the case of an accident, by working with iron; (This likely refers to surgical instruments)
et ne bouter mie ta main en aucun de ces ovraiges tant que tu voies que cist membres soit soffrans celui ovraige.	and do not put your hand to any of these works until you see that this member is able to tolerate that work.
des voines des eulz	of the veins of the eyes
Sebel sont voinnes rouges que sont covertes sus l’oil, et tolent a la veue son ovraige et afoiblissent l’oil toz jors.	Sebel are red veins that cover the eye, and impair vision and weaken the eye constantly.
Mestier est donques au premier que tu regardes se li oil, en coi sebel est, est fors, et n’i a autre maladie fuers que lou sebel;	It is therefore necessary first that you see if the eye, in which the sebel is, is strong, and there is no other disease besides the sebel;
adonques le coil en teil maniere:	then treat it in this manner:
comande au malaide qu’il mette son chief en ton sain, puis sospent celles voines a tout l’oncine selonc sa sapience, et soit li oncines subtilz double selonc ceste forme:	tell the patient to put their head in your lap, then lift these veins with the hook according to your knowledge, and let the hook be subtly double according to this form:
Et soient dui oncine par degrez en I cors selonc ceste forme:	And let there be two hooks by degrees in one body according to this form:
puis c’on coil as forces celles voinnes subtilment, et essue lou sanc houre aprés autre, tant que tu voies removoir celles voines fuers de l’oil;	then when you pull on those veins subtly, and draw out the blood a little at a time, until you see those veins removed from the eye;
et garde que tu ne blecier l’oil as pointes des spatumiles, et fai cest ovraige a houre de midi devant lou soleil, et soies mout fervans en ton ovraige si que tu ne copes fuer que celles voinnes;	and be careful not to injure the eye with the points of the spatulas, and do this work at noon in front of the sun, and be very careful in your work so that you only cut those veins;
et quant tu avras ce fait, si distille en l’oil coliere vert et rouge por corrumpre ceu qui est demorez dou sebel.	and when you have done this, then instill in the eye green and red collyrium to dissolve what remains of the sebel.
Et se tu n’as pooir de coillir tout ceu en celle houre, si fai emplastre sus l’oil de choses apaisans la dolor des eulz, et le laisse aucuns jors tant que li dolors soit apaisie et soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut, puis rencomence selonc ceste maniere qui est devant tant qu’il soit sanez;	And if you are unable to remove all of it at that time, apply a plaster over the eye made of things that soothe eye pain, and leave it for a few days until the pain subsides and a warm abscess is ensured, then start again according to the method described above until it is healed;
et c’est li forme des forces:	and this is the form of the hooks:
de la fistule de l’oil	of the fistula of the eye
Li mire si nomment «arissati» fistule:	Physicians call a fistula "arissati":
quant tu la cures per cautere et par medicine ague ardant selonc ceu que j’ai devant dit, et elle n’est mie sanee, si est engien en li que tu fendes sus l’aposteme, lai ou il doit meurer, et trai toute la moistor que i est, tant que li os soit descovers.	When you treat it with cautery and with a sharp, burning medicine as I have said before, and it is not healed, the method is to cut open the abscess where it should remain, and draw out all the moisture that is there, until the bone is exposed.
Et quant li os iert descovers, et tu verras la corruption et la noiror, si la reis a tout l’estrument de coi ci est li forme;	And when the bone is exposed, and you see the corruption and blackness, then scrape it with the instrument, of which this is the form;
et est apelez «aspre chief», et soit fait de feir inde a I chief reont, et soit pointoiez si com une lime si com il est en la presente forme:	and it is called a "rough head," and it should be made of Indian steel with a round head, and pointed like a file as it is in the present form:
Et met sus lou leu de l’os corrumput, puis le torne entre tes dois, et presse ta main un poc tant que tu saiches que celle corruption est rese;	And place it on the site of the corrupted bone, then turn it between your two fingers, and press your hand a little so that you know that the corruption is scraped;
et fai ceu aucune fois, puis restoure lou leu de medicines exiccatives.	and do this a few times, then restore the area with drying medicines.
se li leus est soudez, et char i naist, et li cors de la bowe est soudez, et remaint ensi XL jors, et il ne renovele et n’est mie apostemez, et accidens mavais n’i vient, saiches qu’il est sanez;	If the place is healed, and flesh grows there, and the body of the boil is healed, and remains so for 40 days, and it does not reopen and is not abscessed, and no bad accident occurs, know that it is healed;
se ceu non, si n’i a autre engien que de ramener la fistule au pertus dou neif selonc ceste forme:	If not, there is no other solution than to bring the fistula back to the opening of the nerve according to this method:
et est que tu descuevre de l’os la seconde fois par fer, et par medicines agues, et quant il iert descovers si prent I foret selonc ceste forme, et soit li chiés de fer a III angles, et li fust soit atenuis jusc’a chief si com tu vois ci:	and that is to uncover the bone a second time with an instrument, and with sharp medicines, and when it is uncovered, take a drill according to this form, and let the head of iron be three-angled, and the shaft be thinned down to the tip as you see here:
puis le met sus l’os delez lou larmier, et esloigne ta main de l’oil I poc, puis torne a tot le foret tant qu’il perce l’os et le sent li malaides par ceu que li vens en ist s’il tient sa main sus son neif;	then place it on the bone next to the tear duct, and move your hand a little away from the eye, then turn the drill completely until it pierces the bone and the patient feels it because the air comes out if he holds his hand over his nerve/nose;
et pues restoure lou leu de medicines seches, si com je t’ai ensigniet, et quant li char naist et endurcist li leus, si vait li matiere au neif;	and then restore the place with dry medicines, as I have taught you, and when the flesh grows and the place hardens, the matter goes to the nerve/nose;
si est plus legiere chose au malaide.	thus it is easier for the patient.
de l’issue de l’oil	of the discharge from the eye
Quant li eulz apert fuer dou tout en tout, et il ne vient point de destorbier au nef, ne amenuisement, si covient que tu lies lou malaide;	When the eye is completely open, and there is no disturbance or lessening to the nose/nerve, then you must tie the patient;
puis le saine, puis li met ventouses ou haterel sens ferir por succier, puis met sus l’oil I liien fait d’acaice et de aloe et d’encens et de sarcocolle, et puis estrain l’oil, et l’emplaustre sus de bendes et de drapelz;	then bleed him, then apply cupping glasses or a tube without lancing to suck, then put on the eye a plaster made of acacia, aloe, incense, and sarcocolla, and then constrict the eye, and the plaster over it with bandages and cloths;
et li maniere des drapelz si est que tu preignes drapelz assez molz, et double chescun en IIII, et puis met l’un sus l’autre selonc la quantiteit que li eulz en ait mestier;	and the method with the cloths is that you take fairly soft cloths, and fold each one in four, and then place one on top of the other according to the quantity the eye needs;
puis l’estrain par desus d’un bendeil dur forment, et rencomence les ventouses por succier sens ferir;	then tighten over it with a very hard bandage, and repeat the cupping glasses to suck without lancing;
puis oste les ventouses et laisse l’oil estraint jor et nuit, et se li liiens amolist, si covient que tu l’estraignes mout;	then remove the cupping glasses and leave the eye constricted day and night, and if the plaster softens, then you must tighten it a lot;
puis oste lou liien aprés le jor et la nut, et se tu vois l’oil repairier, c’est boin;	then remove the plaster after a day and a night, and if you see the eye improving, that's good;
se ce non;	if not;
si rencomence l’emplaustre et les drapelz et lou liien et les ventouses tant qu’il soit sanez.	then repeat the plaster and the cloths and the bandage and the cupping glasses until it is healed.
dou derrompement de toile uvee	of the breaking of the uvea
Quant disruptions vient en la toile uvee, puis apert, et vient fuer des papieres si com I grain de resins, et est espoantauble a veoir;	When a disruption occurs in the uvea, then it opens, and matter comes out of the eyelids like a grain of resin, and it is frightening to see;
adonques se tu la vues coper, li ovraiges est telz que tu boutes une aguille en la racine des la partie desoz jusc’a celi desus, puis boute une autre aguille ou il ait I fil double des la partie dou larmier;	then if you see fit to cut it, the procedure is such that you insert a needle into the root of the part underneath, up to the one above, then insert another needle with a double thread from the corner of the eye;
et la fai percier, et laisse la premiere aguille selonc la disposition;	and pierce it there, and leave the first needle according to the arrangement;
puis cope lou leu dou fil double et lie une partie de l’uve entor, et l’estraint bien, puis estrai l’aguille et met sus l’oil lainne moillie en abun d’uef;	then cut the place of the double thread and tie one part of the uvea around it, and tighten it well, then remove the needle and place wool soaked in egg white on the eye;
et le laisse tant que li filz chiece avec l’uve, puis cure l’oil de choses confortans tant que li plaie soit sanee;	and leave it until the thread falls off with the uvea, then treat the eye with comforting things until the wound is healed;
et aucune fois li plaie est restrainte par l’uve chescune part d’un cercle de drap, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	and sometimes the wound is held together by the uvea, all around, with a circle of cloth, until it is healed.
Et se li eulz done grant apparance, si le perce au spatumile subtil qui viegne em parfont de l’oil, et corre la moistor albuginé et dessende li eulz, et entre ens tantost;	And if the eye swells considerably, pierce it at the thin spot that comes from deep within the eye, and drain the albuginous moisture so the eye goes down, and enter it immediately;
puis l’estrai tant qu’il soit sanez.	then remove it once it is healed.
de la bowe de l’oil	of the swelling of the eye
Ceste maladie qui est apelee «alcunnati» nen est fuers que bowe qui est assemblee en l’oil, semblant a aigue dessendant, et ce n’est mie aigue;	This disease which is called "alcunnati" is nothing but a swelling that has gathered in the eye, resembling dripping water, and yet it is not water;
et li maniere de l’apparance de l’ovraige si est que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege appareilliet et droit, puis prent le chief entre tes mains de II pars, et lou muef tant que tu voies la bowe venir au desus a tes eulz;	and the way to perform the procedure is to have the patient sit on a prepared and straight chair, then take their head in your hands on both sides, and move it until you see the swelling rise up towards your eyes;
puis soit ens fichie, et ne dessende et soit descombree li lumiere, et voie li malaides les choses si com il soloit;	then it should be inserted, so that it does not descend, and the light is unobstructed, and the patient can see things as they used to;
et s’elle ne dessent desoz, saiches que c’est aigue, et se li dessendemens de la bowe n’est appareilliez si com nos avons dit.	and if it does not descend, know that it is water, and the appearance of the swelling is not as we have described.
si fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, puis prent le spatumile subtil et fent sus la toile cornee I poc par la continuation de la conjunctive avec la toile cornee et la corone, tant que li bowe isse;	have the patient sit between your hands, then take a fine spatula and make a small hole in the cornea at the junction of the conjunctiva with the cornea and the iris, so that the swelling comes out;
et quant elle ert issue, si distille en l’oil aigue chaude mellee a miel, ou aigue ou fenugreic est boillis et miel, puis soit curee d’autre cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	and when it has come out, instill warm water mixed with honey into the eye, or water in which fenugreek has been boiled with honey, then treat it with other remedies until it is healed.
des aigues de l’oil	of the waters of the eye
Nos avons jai les semblances des aigues en la division, et ceu qu’il covient por percier;	We have already described the appearances of the waters in the section, and what is necessary for piercing;
si en oevre selonc la santeit.	So act according to the health/condition.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains croisiet, fuers de la lumiere por le soleil, et li lie l’oil sain et estreint mout fort;	You must have the patient sit between your legs crossed, away from the sunlight, and bind the healthy eye and tighten it very firmly;
puis met la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre se li eulz est senestres, ou a ta main destre se li eulz est destres;	then place the eye chart in your left hand if the eye is left, or in your right hand if the eye is right;
puis prent en ta main destre, se li eulz est senestres, l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda», ou a ta main senestre, se li eulz est destre;	then take in your right hand, if the eye is left, the instrument which is called "almagda", or in your left hand, if the eye is right;
puis met la pointe de l’estrument delez la corone par la groissece d’un rait en celle blenchor de l’oil a la partie dou menor larmier, puis boute l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda» vertuousement, et trestorne ta main tant qu’il perce en la blenchor de l’oil, et sente que almagda viegne a la chose vuide;	then place the tip of the instrument next to the pupil about the thickness of a spoke in the white of the eye towards the smaller tear duct, then push the instrument which is called "almagda" forcefully, and twist your hand until it pierces the white of the eye, and feel that the almagda reaches the empty space;
et covient que li mesure de la voie almagda soit au parfont de la mesure des l’espaice qui est des la prunele jusc’a la fin de la noirour;	and the depth of the almagda's path must be equal to the distance from the pupil to the edge of the iris;
et c’est li corone de l’oil;	and that is the pupil of the eye;
si verras l’os en celle papiere por la clarteit de la toile cornee, et pues met l’estrument jusc’a leu ou li aigue est, puis l’espresse desoz une voie aprés autre.	you will see the bone in that spot because of the clarity of the cornea, and then place the instrument up to where the fluid is, then press it out from one path to another.
se li aigue dessent maintenant, si voit li malaides devant lui et l’estrument en son oil.	if the fluid descends immediately, the patient will see in front of him and the instrument in his eye.
Aprés repose I petit, et se li aigue remonte la seconde voie, met la fuer avec l’estrument, et quant elle est ens fichie et ele ne monte, si estrai almagda legierement en tornoiant ta main poc et poc;	Afterwards rest a little, and if the fluid rises again the second time, place the cautery with the instrument, and when it is inserted and it does not rise, then remove the almagda gently by turning your hand little by little;
et puis remette en aigue un poc de seil gemme, et leive de ceu l’oil dedens.	and then put a little bit of rock salt in water, and bathe the eye in this.
Puis met par defuer l’oil estoupes ou lainne moillie en oile roset et en abun d’uef, et lie avec l’oil sain.	Then cover the eye completely with tow or wool soaked in rose oil and egg white, and bandage it with the healthy eye.
Nos, et cil qui sont de nostre tens, mettons sus comin broiet avec abun d’uef.	We, and those who are of our time, apply ground cumin with egg white.
Et se almagda n’i puet entrer en l’oil par sa duresce, car il i a de teilz homes qui ont trop durs les eulz, si covient que tu preignes l’estrument qui est apelez «alberit», de coi ci est li forme:	And if the almagda cannot enter the eye due to its hardness, for there are such men who have very hard eyes, then you must take the instrument which is called "alberit", of which this is the form:
Et perce donques la conjunctive soulement, et n’aler mie trop em parfont, mais fai I leu subtil, puis i boute almagda, si com nos avons dit;	And then pierce the conjunctiva only, and do not go too deep, but make a small hole, then put in the almagda, as we have said;
et au complissement de l’uevre appareille au malaide I dorteur avenant, en coi il dorme sus son dos en I leu tenebrous;	and at the completion of the work, prepare for the patient a suitable dormitory, where he may sleep on his back in a dark place;
et soit deveez de toz movemens, et preigne legieres viandes, et ne mueve son chief ne a destre ne a senestre, et soit liiez selonc sa disposition jusc’a tier jor;	and let him be free from all movements, and take light meals, and not move his head neither to the right nor to the left, and be bandaged according to his condition until the third day;
puis le deslie en cele maison meisme tenebrouse, et esprueve sa veue, et lou fai veoir aucunes choses, et puis li remet lou lien jusc’a septime jor;	then unbind him in that same dark house, and test his sight, and make him see some things, and then reapply the bandage until the seventh day;
et ne covient mie que tu faices ceu en l’oure de la cure ou aprés l’incision maintenant, mais il covient que tu aliges ceu, por ceu que li aigue monte hastanment.	and you should not do this at the time of the treatment or immediately after the incision, but you must delay this, because the humor rises quickly.
se apostemes chaus vient, que tu desliies l’oil devant le septime jor, et l’adrece de ceu qui assouaige aposteme;	If hot abscesses arise, untie the eye before the seventh day and treat it with that which soothes abscesses;
et quant il est apaisiez, si deslie la veue et met sus sa faice I orilliet por covrir aucun jor, et soit adés en celle maison tenebrouse.	and when it is calmed, then uncover the sight and place a pad on his face to cover it for a few days, and he should still be in that dark house.
Et puis isse de la maison poc et poc, et se convertisse en ses cas;	And then he should leave the house little by little, and return to his affairs;
et saiches que nulz deciples ne se doit entremettre en cest cas.	and know that no apprentice should interfere in this case.
Et uns vint a nos qui estoit de la Yrach, qui nos dist que en som pais faisoit om almagda perciet, a coi on succe l’aigue, mais toutevoie je n’en vis onques nul en nostre terre, ne je ne lou lis onques en livres des anciens;	And one came to us who was from Iraq, who told us that in his country they made perforated almond paste through which they sucked water, but nevertheless I never saw any in our land, nor did I ever read about it in the books of the ancients;
et par aventure c’est une novele chose.	and perhaps it is a new thing.
Et ce sont les semblances des formes de almagda, por ceu que cil qui ne les conoit les voie;	And these are the likenesses of the forms of almond paste, so that those who don't know them can see them;
et soient d’arain proprement:	and they should be made of brass specifically:
Et soient li chief d’aus de ceste meisme subtiliteit, et li derriene en III angles ague.	And let their tips be of this same fineness, and the last part in three sharp angles.
de la char sor le neis	of the flesh over the nose
Aucune fois naissent ou neis chars ajostees diverses, de coi il i a aucunes qui semblent scorpions a mout de piez;	Sometimes there arise in the nose diverse fleshy growths, some of which resemble scorpions with many legs;
et si i a de telz ou il ait char enchancree de fuxe color, et si a char souef de bone color.	and there are some where there is flesh ingrained with a pale color, and there is soft flesh of good color.
En celle donques de ces chars qui est souef, et ne mie enchancree, covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains encontre lou soleil;	In the case of the flesh that is soft, and not ingrained, you must have the patient sit between your hands facing the sun;
et oevre ses narines, et giete l’oncine a celles chars, et les trai fuers;	and open his nostrils, and cast the hook at those fleshy growths, and draw them out;
pues cope ceu que tu em pues sostenir au spatumile subtil agut d’une part, tant que tu saiches que celle char est toute ostee.	then cut what you can hold with a thin, sharp spatula on one side, until you know that the flesh is entirely removed.
Et s’il en remaint aucune chose c’on ne puisse coper, si l’ovrez a tout I des estrumens subtil legierement, si qu’il n’i demoure rien;	And if anything remains that cannot be cut, then open it with one of the subtle instruments lightly, so that nothing remains;
et se sans te sormonte, ou aposteme chaus, si lou secort si com il covient;	and if blood overcomes you, or a hot abscess, then treat it as appropriate;
et se c’est apostemes malignes, si te haste et lou cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez et soient ostees toutes les chars, puis giete ou neis aisil et aigue ou vin.	and if it is a malignant abscess, hurry and cauterize it until the bleeding is stopped and all the flesh is removed, then put in clean vinegar and water or wine.
Se li neis oevre, et moistors en vient jusc’a palais, saiches qu’il est sanez;	If the nose opens, and moisture comes down to the palate, know that he is healed;
et se moistors ne perce si com il covient, saiches qu’il i a char nee en l’os desus, a coi li estrumens ne vient mie por taillier:	and if moisture does not flow as it should, know that there is dead flesh on the bone above, which the instrument cannot reach to cut:
adonques covient il que tu i boutes I fil de lin un poc gros, et soit noez de mains nous, et ait entre chescun nout d’espaice I doit ou moins;	then you must put in a rather thick linen thread, knotted by hand, with about a finger's width or less between each knot; 
et mette li malaides lou chiés dou fil en son neif a som pooir, et traie en odorant tant qu’il viegne par lou neif dedens la bouche;	and have the patient put the end of the thread in his nose as far as he can, and pull it while smelling until it comes through the nose into the mouth;
et maintes fois font ensi li enfant as escoles, et c’est legiere chose a celui qui le vuet faire;	and children in schools often do this, and it is an easy thing for anyone who wants to do it;
puis tien le chief qui vient par lou neif a une main, et l’autre chief qui vient par la bouche a l’autre main, et saiche l’un aprés l’autre en soiant as nous qui sont ou fil.	then hold the end that comes through the nose in one hand, and the other end that comes through the mouth in the other hand, and pull one after the other, tugging on the knots that are in the thread.
Fai ceu tant que tu saiches que li nout ont corrompue celle char, puis trai lou filz, essue le sanc, et moille lou fil en oignement egiptien, et le remet derechief au neis si com devant;	Do this until you know that the knots have broken down that flesh, then pull out the thread, wipe the blood, and soak the thread in Egyptian ointment, and put it back in the nose as before;
fai ceu III jors ou plus, tant que li oignemens corrode tout ceu qui est demorez de char;	do this for three days or more, until the ointment corrodes all the remaining flesh;
et puis met ou neis une caine de plonc aucuns jors tant qu’il soit sanez, et s’il a mestier de medicines sechans, si en use;	and then put a lead tube in the nose for a few days until it is healed, and if drying medications are needed, use them;
et c’est li forme de l’estrument por purgier lou chief, a coi on distille les oiles et les medicines ou neis:	and this is the form of the instrument for purging the head, with which oils and medicines are distilled into the nose:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, semblant a une lampe overte, si com une cainne, et li conduis ausi;	And let it be of silver or brass, similar to an open lamp, like a tube, and the conduit likewise;
et se tu vues, si fai une cainne close, et soit li estrumens plains por espurgier lou chief;	and if you wish, make a closed tube, and let the instrument be full to purge the head;
et ait I mainche au chief por lou tenir quant on chaufe l’oile ou aucune liquor.	and it should have a handle at the end to hold it when heating the oil or some liquid.
de la char sor le neis	of the flesh on the nose
Maintes fois naist au chief dou neis une maladie qui est apelee «telul», et croist et devient grans adés, tant qu’il est vis chose au regarder;	Often a disease arises at the tip of the nose which is called "telul," and grows and becomes increasingly large, until it is a hideous thing to look at;
et por ceu covient que tu lou copes au comencement, et l’oste tout fuer, puis met sor leu lou cautere ou la medicine ardant;	and therefore you must cut it at the beginning, and remove it all away, then put on the spot the cautery or the burning medicine;
