Cil donques qui contienent moistor covient qu’il soient copez selonc ceste forme, des la ligne .b. jusc’a la ligne .g.:	Those then that contain moisture must be cut according to this form, from line b. down to line g.:
Et quant toute li bowe qui est en l’aposteme est vuidie, si emple la plaie de viel coton, et la laisse jusc’a l’autre jor, puis oste tout le coton, et cure d’oignement avenant a ceu tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when all the pus that is in the abscess is emptied, then fill the wound with old cotton, and leave it until the next day, then remove all the cotton, and treat with a suitable ointment until it is healed.
Et se li apostemes est de semblances de scrophules, si le fent si com nos avons dit en fendures des scrophules, et se li plaie rent bowe, si amenistre cautere si com nos avons dit devant.	And if the abscess is similar to scrofula, then cut it as we have said in the cutting of scrofula, and if the wound produces pus, then administer a cautery as we have said before.
de la routure de l’artere	Of the rupture of the artery
Quant li artere est route, et li cuir est soudez qui est sus, si en vient maintes fois apostemes, et tout aussi avient il a la voine enflee et aposteme;	When the artery is ruptured, and the skin over it is closed, an abscess often forms, and the same happens with a swollen and abscessed vein;
et si le conoist on ensi quant c’est por l’artere, si est li apostemes lons em parfont;	and it is recognized as being from the artery because the abscess is long and deep;
et quant tu le sens a tes dois, si sens I estraignement;	and when you feel it with your fingers, you feel a tightness;
et quant c’est por la voine, si est reons defuer aparans;	and when it is from the vein, redness from the outside is apparent;
et c’est folie de coper cest aposteme, et meismement quant il est desoz les asseles et as angres et ou col et em mout d’autres leus, et est mout grans.	and it is foolish to cut open this abscess, especially when it is under the armpits, in the groin, or on the neck, and in many other places, and is very large.
Il covient donques eschuir la cure de fer, et celui qui est a chief covient eschuir ausi, et en celui qui est d’enfleure d’artere fent par desus le cuir dou lonc;	It is therefore necessary to avoid the iron cure, and the one at the head must also be avoided, and in the one that is a swelling of an artery, make an incision along the length above the skin;
puis oevre la taille as oncines, et depart bellement l’artere des toiles, tant qu’ele soit descoverte;	then open the incision with hooks, and carefully separate the artery from the tissues until it is exposed;
puis boute desoz li une aguille, et la fai percier jusc’a l’autre costeit, et estraint l’artere d’un fil double en II leus, selonc ceu que je t’ai ensigniet en l’estraction des II arteres qui sont en temples;	then place a needle under it, and make it pierce through to the other side, and tie off the artery with a double thread in two places, as I have taught you in the extraction of the two arteries that are in the temples;
puis point le leu qui est entre les II liens d’un intromissoire tant que li sans en isse qui i est, et soit deliiez li aposteme;	then puncture the area between the two ties with a lancet so that the blood that is there comes out, and the abscess is drained;
puis amenistre la cure que enjanre bowe, tant que li liien chient;	then administer the treatment that causes healing by suppuration, until the ligatures fall off;
puis cure ceu d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then treat it with a suitable ointment, until it is healed;
et se li apostemes est por la taille de la voinne, si covient que tu teignes a ta main ceu que tu pues de l’aposteme a tout le cuir, puis boute l’aguille desoz le leu que tu tiens a ta main, et la fai percier, et i ait I fil double, si que tu le trais de l’autre costeit;	and if the abscess is because of the cutting of the vein, then you must hold in your hand as much of the abscess as you can, along with the skin, then put the needle under the place that you hold in your hand, and make it pierce through, and have a double thread there, so that you pull it to the other side;
puis lie l’aposteme, si com je t’ai dit, ou liien de l’une de II pars as II chiés dou fil;	then tie off the abscess, as I told you, with a ligature on one of the two sides with the two ends of the thread;
et se tu doutes que li filz n’isse fuer, si i reboute une autre aguille a tout I fil desoz tout l’aposteme a l’incision de la premiere aguille, et estraint les filz en IIII leus;	and if you are worried that the thread might come out, then put another needle with a thread under the whole abscess at the incision point of the first needle, and secure the threads in four places;
puis cope l’aposteme tant que li superfluitez en isse, puis cope la superfluiteit dou keur et laisse ceu qui est liiez;	then cut the abscess so that the excess comes out, then cut the excess flesh and leave what is tied;
puis met sus I drapeil moilliet en vin et en oile, puis li amenistre cures de tentes et d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	then put on a cloth moistened with wine and oil, then administer treatments with tents and ointments until it is healed.
des apostemes des ners	of abscesses of the nerves
Ausi com aposteme vienent en l’artere et en la voine, vienent aposteme as ners quant il sont ferut, ou par trop grant travail, et semblans choses.	Just as abscesses occur in the artery and in the vein, abscesses occur in the nerves when they are injured, or by excessive work, and similar things.
Et ceu avient plus sovent as adjutoires et as dois et en toz leus ou il ait jointures, et c’est I grief apostemes, et sa color semble la color dou cors, et est em plusors dispositions sens dolor;	And this occurs more often in the shoulders and in the fingers and in all places where there are joints, and it is a serious abscess, and its color resembles the color of the body, and it is in several forms without pain;
et quant on l’estraint forment, si sent li malaides dolor, et n’est mie em parfont dou cors, mais desoz lou keur;	and when it is pressed firmly, the patient feels pain, and it is not deep in the body, but under the skin;
et muet bien de toutes pars, et ne va ne avant ne arrier, ne desoz ne desus, et celui qui est en jointures ne covient mie coper par fer:	and moves easily in all directions, and goes neither forward nor backward, nor below nor above, and the one that is in the joints should not be cut with iron:
par aventure i vanroit contraction;	by chance, contraction would occur there;
et cil qui est ou chief ou ou front, fent le cuir au spatumile.	and the one that is on the head or on the forehead, cut the skin with a spatula.
Se li apostemes est petis, si le tien a unes tenailles, et le cope en sa racine;	If the abscess is small, hold it with tweezers/forceps and cut it at its root;
et s’il est grans, si le sospent a l’oncine, et l’escorche, puis l’oste et assemble la plaie a la costure, et lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and if it is large, suspend it with a hook, and peel it, then remove it and bring the wound together with stitching, and treat it until it is healed.
des grosses boces pendans	of the large hanging lumps/swellings/goiters
Aucune fois avient en ventres et ne mie autre part thelul, et est une maladie qui est apelee «funge» par la semblance d’aus, et est li racine subtilz, et li chiez gros;	Sometimes a thelul occurs in the belly and nowhere else, and it is a disease which is called "fungus" because of its resemblance to them, and its root is thin, and its head large;
et en i a de petis et de mout grans;	and there are some small and some very large;
et je vis I home qui en avoit II ou ventre qui estoient plus semblans a funges que ai autre chose, et n’i avoit point de difference, et estoient blanc, et avoient menue racine, et estoient jai fendut, et en corroit adés moistor.	and I saw a man who had two in his belly that looked more like fungi than anything else, and there was no difference, and they were white, and they had a slender root, and they had already split open, and moisture constantly flowed from them.
Je les copai et trovai en l’un XVIII onces pesant, et en l’autre VI З., et li ovraiges en l’incision si est que tu regardes se li malaides est moistes, et li color de l’artelul est blainche et moiste et de subtil racine;	I cut them out and found in one eighteen ounces in weight, and in the other six and a half, and the procedure for the incision is that you consider if the patient is moist/phlegmatic, and the color of the growth is white and moist and with a thin root;
si le cope au spatumile large, et soient en ta presence li cautere au feu.	then cut it with a wide spatula, and have the fire cauteries ready at hand.
Car au taillier vient maintes fois trop grans decorremens de sanc, et se li sans te vaint, si te haste donques dou cauterizer;	For during the cutting, excessive bleeding often occurs, and if the blood overcomes you, then hurry to cauterize;
et se tu vois le malaide espoanteit et paourous de l’incision dou fer, si prent I fil de plonc bien fait, et en lie l’artelul si com nos avons dit, et le laisse II jors;	and if you see the patient frightened and afraid of the incision with the iron, then take a well-made lead wire, and tie off the growth as we have said, and leave it for two days;
et puis le restraint, et ne cesser d’estraindre lou fil de plonc tant qu’il cope l’artelul, et chiece par lui sens travail;	and then tighten it, and do not stop tightening the lead wire until it cuts through the growth, and it falls off by itself without difficulty;
et se les racines sont grosses, si a paour au coper meismement por le ventre, mais tu em pues bien coper la moitiet, puis le cauterize qu’il ne reviegne;	and if the roots are large, be careful when cutting, especially near the abdomen, but you can safely cut away half of it, then cauterize it so it does not grow back; 
puis cure la plaie, et garde que tu ne coper le thelul qui est de fuxe color et de povre sens et de lait regart.	then treat the wound, and be careful not to cut the swelling which has a pale color and little feeling and a milky appearance.
Car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, et je venrai a la cure de chancre ci aprés.	For this is a cancerous abscess, and I will come to the treatment of cancer later.
quant li boude ist fuer	when the intestine protrudes outside
Se li apparance de la boude vient par cautere de plaie ou de fendure de syfac, et est sus le ventre et en ist aucuns des bouez, si com il avient en autres routures, ou de sanc qui cort de voines ou d’arteres selonc ceu qui est devant, ou de ventositeit;	If the appearance of the intestine comes from a cauterized wound or a ruptured syfac (intestinal abscess/fistula), and it is on the abdomen and some of the intestines protrude, as it happens in other ruptures, or from blood flowing from veins or arteries depending on what is in front, or from flatulence; 
et se c’est par la routure dou syfac et par l’issue dou bouel, si est li color de l’aposteme semblans a la color dou cors, et est legiere chose sens dolor, et apert de diverse issue.	and if it is through the rupture of the syfac and through the exit of the intestine, then the color of the abscess is similar to the color of the body, and it is a light thing without pain, and it appears with various openings.
Et se c’est por l’issue de l’intestine, adonques est il plus divers, et quant on le presse a ses dois si se repont, et puis revient, et par aventure si est sarrez, et agrandist mout a l’entree dou bain et por fort travail.	And if it is due to the protrusion of the intestine, then it is more varied, and when one presses it with their fingers, it withdraws, and then returns, and perhaps it is constricted, and greatly enlarges upon entering the bath and from strong exertion.
Et se c’est por moistor, c’est legiere chose, et apert bien quant tu le presses a ta main, ne ne constraint mie;	And if it is due to moisture, it is a light thing, and it is readily apparent when you press it with your hand, and it is not constricted;
et se c’est por sanc, si apert par ces signes li apostemes gros et dur, et est fichiez selonc une quantiteit;	and if it is due to blood, the abscess appears by these signs: large and hard, and fixed in a certain area;
et se c’est por ventositeit, si est souef au tochier, et li ovraiges si est que tu regarde se li apparance est por le sanc de l’artere, ou de la voine, ou ventositeit.	and if it is due to flatulence, it is soft to the touch, and the task is to see if the appearance is due to blood from an artery, or a vein, or flatulence.
Si covient que tu laisses la cure.	Then you must abandon the treatment.
Car il en a doutance et paor, si com je t’ai dit ou chapistre des apostemes, por l’artere et por la voine.	For there is doubt and fear, as I told you in the chapter on abscesses, concerning the artery and the vein.
Et se li apparance est por l’intestine ou lou boueil, si covient que tu comandes au malaide qu’il teigne son alaine, et soit estendus tout drois, puis seigne d’enche tout entor la boude;	And if the appearance is due to the intestine or the bowel, then you must instruct the patient to hold their breath, and lie stretched out straight, then mark with ink all around the swelling;
puis le comande a gesir sovin entre tes mains, puis va entor le leu que tu as signiet a tout le spatumile, puis estent la moitiet de l’aposteme au desus a tout le grant uncine;	then have them lie face down between your hands, then go around the area you marked with the spatula, then spread half of the abscess above with the large hook;
puis le lie entor d’un fil fort, ou d’une corde de fort soie fermement, et soit li nous dou liien assolz;	then tie it around with a strong thread, or a cord of strong silk firmly, and let the knot of the tie be loose;
puis oevre la moitiet de l’aposteme estendut sus le liien, et i boute ton doit indice, et quier l’intestine;	then open the half of the abscess spread over the tie, and put your index finger in it, and search for the intestine;
se tu le trueves pris dou liien, si le deslie, et boute l’intestine au defuer dou ventre;	if you find it caught in the tie, untie it, and push the intestine back inside the belly;
et se tu trueves le boueil, si le prent a l’oncine, et en cope la superfluiteit;	and if you find the swelling, take it with the hook, and cut off the excess;
et se li artere te fait contraire, ou li voine, si vai belement entor, puis revien a ton ovraige et pren II aguilles, et i boute II fors filz, et boute les II aguilles entor ceu que tu as fait en crois que tu feis percier;	and if the artery or vein gives you trouble, go around it carefully, then return to your work and take two needles, and thread two strong threads through them, and place the two needles around what you have done in a cross so that you make them pierce [the tissue];
puis estrain l’aposteme en IIII leus sus les aguilles, et se tu vues, oste les aguilles, et laisse lou leu tant qu’il porrisse, et chiece li char morte par soi;	then tighten the abscess in four places over the needles, and if you wish, remove the needles, and leave the area until it rots, and the dead flesh falls off by itself;
ou tu la cope quant elle iert subtiliie et porrie, puis le cure de ceu qu’il covient, et cheve l’aposteme si com nos avons dit;	or you cut it when it is thinned and rotted, then treat it as appropriate, and shave the abscess as we have said;
et estrai le sanc ou la moistor que tu trueves, puis cure le leu de ceu qu’il couvient, et soude le leu.	and remove the blood or moisture that you find, then treat the area appropriately, and suture the area.
dou chancre	of the canker/ulcer
Nos avons dit en la division les semblances de chancre, et coment on i doit ovrer par medicines, et coment on doit eschuer la cure de fer;	We have spoken in the division about the appearances of a canker/ulcer, and how one should work on it with medicines, and how one should avoid treatment with iron/surgery;
et disons le chancre enjanreit en la marris, et grant cautele a en la cure, et dirent li ancien que quant chancres est en leu ou on le puet raier si com chancre qui est em mameles, et en la cuixe, et en semblans leus, et le doit tout oster quant il est en l’encomencement;	and we say the canker/ulcer degenerates into necrosis, and great caution is needed in the treatment, and the ancients said that when a canker/ulcer is in a place where it can be scraped, like a canker/ulcer that is in the breasts, and in the thigh, and in similar places, it should be completely removed when it is in the beginning;
et quant il est grans et anciens, si ne covient mie que tu l’aproches, car je n’en poi onques nul saner;	and when it is large and old, you should not approach it, because I have never been able to heal any;
ne nulz n’en sana onques devant moi.	nor has anyone ever healed one before me.
Et li ovraiges, quant il est en leu ou on le puet oster, si com nos avons dit, est que tu purge aucune fois le malaide de cole noire;	And the procedure, when it is in a place where it can be removed, as we have said, is that you sometimes purge the patient of black bile;
puis le fai sainier s’il ait manifeste repletion, puis afaite le malaide I boin leu por faire l’ovraige;	then have them bled if there is manifest plethora, then prepare the patient in a good place to perform the procedure;
puis giete tes oncines ou chancre, et le cheve de toutes pars, et l’oste de toutes pars sens rien laissier;	then cast your hooks or pincers, and pull it from all sides, and remove it completely without leaving anything behind;
et laisse corre le sanc tout fuer, et espreint bien le leu a ta main ou a aucune chose, et se li decorremens de sanc te fait contraire de l’incision de l’artere ou de la voine, si le cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	and let the blood flow freely, and press the area well with your hand or something else, and if the flow of blood prevents you from incising the artery or vein, cauterize it until the bleeding is stopped;
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it with other remedies until it is healed.
de ydropisie	of dropsy
Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer:	We have already discussed in the division the different types of dropsy, and how the accumulation of water occurs, and the signs of each type, and the treatment that is done with medicines, and that which is treated with iron:
si est eclites soulement;	if it is only superficial;
et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces II semblances:	and one should not touch with iron in these two types:
c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose;	that is to say, tympanites and ascites, because it is a fatal thing;
donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses;	Therefore, when you treat this type of dropsy which is called "anasarca" with medicines, and the treatment is not effective, then see if the patient is weak, or if they have another illness besides dropsy, such as coughing and diarrhea and similar things;
si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance;	do not touch it with iron, because there is danger;
et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer:	and if you see the patient is of strong constitution, and they have no other illness than just dropsy, and they are not too young nor too old, then you should proceed as follows:
lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme:	Lift the patient upright with your hands, and an assistant should press the belly, pushing the water to the lowest part of the abdomen, then take the thorned spatula made in this way:
Et soit trenchans de II pars.	And let it be sharp on both sides.
a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier;	with a point, and yet not so penetrating that it can reach the intestine when inserted, and not be able to wound it; 
puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines:	then see if the dropsy originates from near the intestines:
si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude III dois droit desoz sus lou poignil;	then you must cut above the navel three fingers directly below, towards the pubic bone;
et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude III dois;	and if the dropsy is due to liver disease, let your incision be three fingers to the left of the navel;
et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu;	and if it's because of the spleen, let it be on the right, and the patient should not lie on the incision so that the excess fluids don't flow to that weak spot;
puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor;	then pierce all the skin with the instrument, push it in, and lift your hand with the spatula between the skin and the superficial fascia as if skinning, about the size of a fingernail or thereabouts;
puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme:	then pierce the superficial fascia until the spatula reaches the empty space, and that is the location of the fluid, then pull it out, and insert this instrument of which here is the form:
Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz I petit pertus;	And it is similar to a thin silver tube, and it is made of light brass or bronze, and has a small hole in the lower part;
et ou costeit d’une part, III pertus;	and on one side, three holes;
et II d’autre part, et I d’autre;	and two on the other side, and one on the other;
et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:	and the head is cut like a pen, and this is the shape of the incision with which the scribe cuts the pen:
au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument;	at the top is the wing, so that when the instrument comes to the point, it immediately descends onto the instrument;
vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort;	then empty half or a third, for if you empty more than is necessary at that time, perhaps the patient will die from the release of his spirit from the soul, or he will faint, or he will approach death;
mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz;	but empty it according to the quantity of his strength, and according to what the dispositions of the patient's strength indicate, and his pulse;
puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere;	then withdraw the instrument and hold the needle, and it is held immediately by the core that plugs the hole that is on the syfac, of which I have spoken, which you pierce in this way; 
puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit;	then start the instrument again the next day, if you see the patient tolerating it, and draw out a small amount of fluid;
fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue.	do this for a few days, and be careful not to drain so much that nothing remains but a small amount of fluid. 
Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre;	And if you are concerned about the patient, and you leave a lot of fluid, treat him with burial in warm sand, and with much sweating or baths and in the sun, and let him abstain from drinking;
et le cure de medicines desiccatives tant qu’il soit sanez, et cauterize sus l’estomac et sus lou foie et sus l’esplen aprés l’estraction de l’aigue, si com j’ai dit devant.	and treat him with drying medicines until he is healed, and cauterize over the stomach and over the liver and over the spleen after the extraction of the fluid, as I have said before.
de l’estopement de la verge	On the blockage of the penis/membrum
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu.	Sometimes children are born without an opening in the penis, or the opening is small, or it is not in the right place.
Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout I spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme:	So it is necessary to pierce it immediately with a very fine spatula according to this form/method:
puis met ou pertus I clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi III jors ou IIII et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet;	Then put in the opening a fine nail of lead, and tie it and keep it thus for three or four days and when he needs to urinate, the nail should be removed, and let him urinate, and then replace it;
et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	and perhaps it is not necessary, because the urine that comes out will not let it close.
Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s’eslargera.	He whose opening is small, is treated with the lead nail, as we have said, so it will widen.
Cil qui n’ont mie le pertus en lor leu sont bleciet, car aucun naissent qui ont le pertus au chief de la verge, por coi il ne puient pissier avant s’il ne lievent lor verge en haut;	Those who do not have the opening in its proper place are injured, for some are born with the opening at the tip of the penis, so they cannot urinate forward unless they raise their penis up;
et ne pueent enjanrer por ceu que li matiere ne puet venir jusc’a la marris, et c’est une male maladie.	and cannot procreate because the semen cannot reach the vagina, and this is a bad condition.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient;	And the method of the procedure is that the patient lies on his back, then you extend the tip of the penis and cut it like the width of a quill, so that the opening falls in the middle, as it should;
et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s’il avient, si l’estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu’il soit sanez.	and beware of bleeding which often occurs there, and if it happens, staunch it with something that stops blood, and treat the wound until it is healed.
des pustules de la verge	of pustules of the penis
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide;	Many times these sores appear on the penis, and it is an appearance of ugly flesh;
et en i a malignes et non malignes;	and some are malignant and some are not malignant; (or, and there are malignant ones and non-malignant ones)
si covient que tu les preignes a I oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien;	so you should take them with a fine hook, and cut and clean them all, then apply cotton moistened with Egyptian ointment;
puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it with diafinicon ointment until it is healed.
Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere.	And if the sore is malignant, of a foul color and suppurating, then you must apply cautery to it.
Quant tu l’as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l’albathe qui est dedens premier;	When you have cut it, and if the ulcer is at the tip of the penis, and part of it is inside the skin and part outside, you must first remove the ulcer that is inside; 
et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer.	and when it is stitched up, then treat the outside.
Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion;	For when you treat it all together, the head of the penis is not protected from being pierced, and blackness and corruption comes into the penis and into the testicle;
si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	so it is necessary to remove everything that is black and corrupted, then apply a plaster of honey and flour made from pomegranate peel and vetches, then treat it with other remedies until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme:	And if bleeding occurs, apply the lunar cautery in this way:
Li cauteres si aide as II dispositions ensamble:	The cautery helps with both conditions together:
c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption;	that is, the bleeding and the corruption;
et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi;	and if the head of the penis is corrupted and retracted, you must insert a lead tube into the urethra, and the patient should urinate through it;
et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a I estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars;	and when the skin is tight at the head of the penis, which happens to those who have not been circumcised, or it occurs due to a wound or an abscess, then you must peel it back with a pointed instrument, until the ligament is loosened, and the head of the penis is freed on all sides;
et se c’est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l’escorches a I spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil;	and if it is difficult to separate this, then you must peel it back with a spatula a little from the head of the penis and the skin;
puis dessevre belement entre II, et i met I subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu’il n’aerse derechief.	then gently separate the two, and insert a thin linen cloth soaked in cold water, so that it doesn't tighten again.
de la circoncision	of circumcision
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies;	Circumcision is not a separation of continuity like other wounds;
toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	however, when we perform this procedure by choice, specifically on children, it is necessary that we do the best work, and the most conducive to healing.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not speak of the circumcision of their children, for it was not practiced in their law, and we have only what we have learned through experience.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor I dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule;	For I have seen the majority of masters and healers perform circumcision around the first day, forcefully, and with a razor;
si fuioit li keurs car il i a II toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	thus the skin fled, for there are two layers, and by chance they would cut the upper one and leave the one below.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre;	Then it was necessary to cut it again, and the pain was doubled, and during the cleansing, which takes place on the eighth day, the tip of the member is not safe;
et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	and during the cleansing of the nail, by chance the iron slips, and they ruin the work, and often they are born such that they do not need cleansing and I have seen it.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	Regarding the cleansing which is done forcefully with a linen thread, I have found the experiment to be good, for the threads cut evenly both above and below.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en I tout soul tens;	For when you squeeze your hand, you cut evenly in a single instant;
mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir;	but the thread must be tightly wrapped around the skin;
et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues;	and the way of the first procedure is that you make the child think, if he understands, that you are only tying the thread around the penis, and then you make him happy in all the ways you can;
puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens;	then have him stand straight between your hands, and hide the threads between your hands or under your feet so that the child cannot see them, nor any of the instruments;
puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens;	then put your hand on the penis and blow in the opening, and pull it upwards until the glans of the penis is inside;
puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz I poc a I autre liien;	then clean it well of the dirt that has accumulated there, then tie the marked place with a double thread, then tie it below, a little further down, with another tie;
et la tien as II dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les II liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge;	and hold it with two fingers by the second tie with the thumb and index finger, and cut between the two ties, then quickly lift the glans and pull the tip of the penis;
puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres;	then let the blood flow little by little, because that is the best;
et met poudre sus et sus la poudre I drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and put powder on it and over the powder a cloth soaked in a mixture of cooked egg yolk diluted with rose water, blended with good fresh rose oil, and leave it on until the next day, and treat it with other treatments until it is healed.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste:	The method of strengthening for cleansing is this:
li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	The two edges should be thin and sharp, and the edges should be as wide as the handle equally:
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision;	The error of cleansing is when the core inside escapes the incision;
donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme;	Then you must expand it with your fingernail, before the place forms an abscess;
et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	and cut it evenly, and if you cannot hold it with your fingernail, hold it with forceps, and then cut it.
Et s’il trespassent III jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement;	And if it goes beyond three days, and what is under the penis is swollen, leave it until the hot abscess is subsided, and peel it lightly;
si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	cut it as best you can, and be careful of the part of the penis, it will not harm it at all.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point;	Then treat the area with wound-healing powders, as we have described in the section on powders, and if one cuts from the heart excessively, and it goes above, it will not cause harm;
cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	treat it then, as we have said, until it is healed.
dou retenement de l’urine	of urinary retention
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	Urinary retention is caused by a blockage from a stone, or congealed blood, or pus, or dead flesh, or similar things, as we have said in the classification;
et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz;	and if the urine is not released, and you see that the retention is due to a stone which is located at the neck of the bladder, then the patient must be bent over his knees;
et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet;	and his feet should be placed on his back, and extend his belly from the top toward his back, and the patient should hold his breath as much as he can;
et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e;	and then the neck of the bladder is forced to expel the stone upwards, which allows the urine to be released; 
et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme:	and if it does not come out, as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, then you must administer extraction with the instrument called "syringe," of which this is the form:
et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil;	and it should be made of thin, light silver, shaped like a bird's feather;
et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	and the cannula should be a palm and a half long, and thin at the end.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue;	And the way to release the urine is this: you take a double thread, and tie a small piece of wool or cotton to the end, and put the end of the thread inside the syringe;
et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede;	and cut the excess wool and push it up to the end of the syringe, then anoint the syringe with oil or butter and egg white, and have the patient sit on a seat, and sprinkle the bladder and penis with warm oil and olive oil and lukewarm water;
puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude;	then gently insert the syringe into the penis, until it reaches the base of the penis, then bend the penis over towards the buttocks;
puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors;	then push the syringe forward to the bladder, and the patient will feel it reach the empty space, and this is not done according to this order except because the passage where it goes is twisted;
puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine;	then pull the thread with the wool little by little, and the urine will follow the wool, then pull it out, and let the urine flow;
et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	and reinsert the syringe until the bladder is emptied, and the patient is relieved.
des maladies de la vessie	of bladder diseases
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When excoriations or blood appear in the bladder, or pus has collected there, and you want to instill waters and medicines, then make the instrument that is called "clepsydra", and this is its form:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus:	It is closed, and has three holes:
II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois;	Two on one side, and one on the other, as you see;
et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;	and the nozzle end through which the medicine flows should be such that it fits tightly into the penis without anything added, so that one can draw out the moisture, and inject when necessary;
et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens;	and when you want to pour your medicines into the bladder, place the end of the catheter in the liquid, and draw on the suction device that is inside;
si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens;	thus you will draw the moisture into the catheter, and then push the suction device back in firmly;
si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;	so the liquid will enter and go directly to the bladder, so that the patient will feel it;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie:	and this is the form of the thin clyster with which one irrigates the bladder:
si est ci:	so it is here:
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut;	And it is made of silver or brass, and the head is higher up;
et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet;	and underneath has a cavity where the liquid falls;
puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu;	then take a sheep's bladder and put in it the liquid with which you want to irrigate the bladder, then tie it firmly between the two cavities with a good double thread, and warm this liquid a little over the fire;
puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;	then insert the tip of the clyster into the penis, then squeeze your hand on the bladder evenly with the liquid, until the patient feels that the liquid has reached the bladder;
et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor;	and if you don't have a bladder, then take a piece of parchment and make a circle out of it, and pierce it all around; 
puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument;	then thread a strong string through these holes, then gather the circle as one gathers a bag, and put inside what you want of oil and liquid and water, and tie it to the instrument;
et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	and do as you did with the bladder, squeezing with your hand until the liquid reaches the bladder.
de la piere	of the stone
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines;	We have already spoken, in the section on types of stones, and their extraction, along with medications;
et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille;	and have explained the difference between the stone generated in the kidneys, and all the signs, and in which stone one should operate surgically;
et en la vessie, et en la verge;	and in the bladder, and in the penis;
et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	and I will tell you plainly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit;	I say that the stone which is generated in the bladder occurs more often in children, and it is a sign that the liquid coming from the bladder resembles water in its clarity; 
et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist;	and sand appears in it, and the patient scratches his penis, and it hangs down often, and then hardens;
et a mout de ces saut li fondemens;	and he has a lot of these discharges from the bladder;
et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont IIII ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece;	and the healing of children is easy until they are four years old, and is very difficult in old men, and is moderate in young men, for those who are between youth and old age;
et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	and the cure is easier for those who have large stones than for those who have small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	And when we come to the treatment, it is first necessary to cleanse the patient with an enema, to remove all the feces that are in the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	For it sometimes hinders the search for the stone.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut;	Then take the patient by the feet, and shake him and move him downward, so that the stone descends to the bottom of the bladder, and sometimes jumps up from the high place;
puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval;	then have him sit prepared between your hands, and his hands should be under his thighs, so that the bladder is completely inclined downwards;
puis la quier et la touche dedens;	then search for it and touch it inside;
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	if you feel the stone in the space, then hurry now to cut on the stone.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis;	And if it does not fall at the touch at all, wet your index finger with oil, of the left hand, if the patient is a child, or your middle finger if the patient is a fully grown youth;
et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie;	and put it in his anus, and search for the stone, and when you feel it with your finger, guide it to the neck of the bladder;
puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	then press down with your finger, and push it outside where you intend to cut.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille;	And instruct the assistant to press the bladder with his hand, and tell him to lift the testicles upwards with his right hand, and with his left hand to pull back the skin which is beneath the testicles in the area where one makes the incision;
puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	then place there the cutting spatula, of which this is the form:
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre;	And cut between that which is between the testicles and the anus, not in the middle but to the side of the left buttock;
et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;	and be directly over the stone, and keep your fingers always in the anus, and make the incision transverse so that it is wide on the outside, and narrow within, according to the size of the stone, not too large;
par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail;	perhaps press it with the finger that is in the anus, so that it may leap out without difficulty;
et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges:	and know that there are some stones with angles and edges:
si est griés a issir;	thus it is difficult to extract;
et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	and there are some that are smooth, resembling an acorn, and round, whose extraction is easy.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant;	In the case of those that have angles and edges, make the incision larger;
et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe;	and if it does not jump out, you must then tighten the forceps that are like a file at the end, to firmly grasp the stone so that it does not escape;
ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief;	or you insert underneath it a subtle instrument curved at the end;
et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;	and if you cannot manipulate it thus, widen the opening a little, and if the blood flows, staunch it with vitriol;
et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	and if there is more than one stone, first push the largest to the neck of the bladder, then cut down on it, then pull it out, and the smaller ones afterward if there are several.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	And if it is very large, it must be sawn, and a larger incision made.
Car II choses avienent au malaide:	For two things happen to the patient:
ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder;	either he dies, or the urine constantly flows from there so the area cannot heal;
mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;	but nevertheless strive to pull it out, or break it up with forceps, until you remove it piece by piece;
et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut;	and when you have completed your work, fill the wound with frankincense and aloe and dragon's blood, and bind it, and put over it a cloth moistened with oil and wine, or with oil and rose water and cold water, to soothe the hot abscess;
puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	then turn the patient onto his back, and do not loosen the bandage until the third day.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you untie it, wash the area very well with oil and water, then treat it with diachylon ointment and basilicon ointment, until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine:	And if hot abscesses come in the wound and corrosion, and clotting of blood in the bladder, and because of this the urine is retained, which is recognized in such a way that blood comes with the urine:
boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit;	then put your finger in the wound, and extract that blood, for if it remains there, it will corrode the bladder, and rot it;
puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then wash the wound with water and vinegar and salt, and help him in all the ways you know, until he is healed;
et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	and it is necessary that every time you treat him, that you tie his two thighs together, and apply the medicines on the area.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir;	And if the stone is small, and it is in the urethra, and stuck there, and the urine cannot come out;
si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	if you treat it with what I mentioned before, that you cut him many times, one is excused from cutting due to this treatment.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	I have already proven this.
Pren I foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a III angles fichiees en I tison:	Take an iron drill of this shape and let it be three-sided, stuck in a firebrand:
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie;	then take a thread and tie it around the penis below the stone, so that it cannot go back into the bladder;
puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere;	then insert the drill into the penis lightly, until it reaches the stone;
et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part;	and turn the drill with your hand into the stone little by little, until you can pierce the stone on the other side;
si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	then the urine will come immediately, then press your hand on what remains of the stone that is inside the penis.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	It is immediately broken, and comes out with the urine, and the patient is healed;
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie;	and if you cannot do this for any reason that prevents it, then tie one thread below the stone and another above, then cut the penis at the location of the stone between the two threads, then pull it out, and untie the thread, and clean the congealed blood that is in the wound;
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat it until it is healed.
de la piere des femmes	of the stone of women
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por III choses:	It rarely happens that a stone is generated in women, and if it does happen sometimes, then the treatment is difficult, and is problematic for three reasons:
l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge;	the first is that perhaps the woman is a virgin;
et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	and the second is that one cannot find a knowledgeable woman who will reveal herself to doctors, especially when she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains;	And the third reason is that perhaps one cannot find a woman skilled in this manual art;
et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil;	and the fourth reason is that the woman's stone is deeper than the man's stone, which is why it requires a deeper cut, and there is great fear. And if necessity compels this, then you must take a very knowledgeable midwife, and they are hardly found, and if you don't find one, then seek a chaste and subtle physician;
et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	and present her a wise matron, experienced in the lives of women, or a woman who knows some of the art, and instruct her to do what you command regarding the examination of the stone;
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge:	and look carefully to see if the woman is a virgin:
adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere;	then she must insert her finger into the rectum and search for the stone;
et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	and if she finds it, she should hold it under her finger, and instruct the patient to insert her finger into her vagina, and search and press firmly with her left hand on the bladder.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse;	If she finds it, she should move it little by little from the entrance of the bladder downwards, until it comes to the root of the thigh;
puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie;	then cut down on the stone at the root of the thigh opposite the middle of the vulva, where it is prepared and soft, and feel the stone in that area;
et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	and don't move her finger from above or below the stone, and let the incision at first be small;
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont:	then insert the hook into the incision, if you feel the stone then enlarge the wound until the stone can come out, and know that there are many kinds of stones:
c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	that is to say, small and large and rough and smooth, long and round, and those that have branches.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	so know the appearances in order to understand the outcome.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if the blood overcomes you, apply ground vitriol to the place, and hold it for an hour until the blood is stanched;
puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	then return to your work, until the stone is out, and have the instruments that I told you about in the extraction of stones in men to help you in your work;
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide;	and if the blood overcomes you, and it is from the artery that is cut, put the powder on the place and bind it with tents and bandages, and do not start this again, and leave the stone and do not pull it out, because perhaps the patient would die;
puis cure la plaie.	then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood is calmed, and the place festers, then return to your work, until the stone is out.
de hernie carnouse	of fleshy hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef;	Aqueous hernia is nothing other than a collection of moisture or white syfac, which is below the shell of the testicles, that contains the testicle;
et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit I autre oef;	and is called "syfac", and sometimes it is actually within the lining of the testicle, so that one thinks it is another testicle;
et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit;	and it is the skin of the scrotum between the white syfac that we have mentioned;
et ceu n’avient se poc non.	and this occurs infrequently.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the development of this hernia comes from weakness in the testicles, and this matter is spread.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors:	And sometimes it comes from a blow to the testicles, and this fluid has many colors:
ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	either a color tending towards jaundice, or it is blood red, or black, or watery white, and this occurs more often;
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	and these are the signs to recognize this gathering, for if it is in the white syfac (hydrocele) that we have mentioned, the abscess is round, a little long like the shape of an egg, and the testicle is not visible, because there is fluid all around it.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	And if there is fluid in the tunic itself, the abscess is round with part of the testicle, and because of this, it is thought to be another testicle;
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien;	and if the fluid is between the skin of the testicles and the white tunic, it can be felt easily;
donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	then when you want to know the color of the fluid, examine it with the square intromissor, the shape of which is shown above.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	According to what comes out after the intromissor, judge what is inside.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors;	And when we treat it with iron (cautery), the patient should be bled according to his strength and the fullness of his body;
puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	then have him lie on his back, on something slightly raised, and place many cloths under him;
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions;	then sit on his left, and instruct the assistant to sit on the right, and extend the penis to one of the two testicles from the heart of the scrotum;
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	then take the milk-white spatula, and cut the skin of the scrotum lengthwise from the base to near the tip, and let your incision be perfectly straight, dividing the skin of the scrotum down to the white tunic, and peel it back subtly as much as possible;
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont;	then pierce the tunic full of water with a large hole, and draw out all the water, then insert your hooks and stretch the tunic upwards;
et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement;	and do not touch the testicle itself, only the tunic;
cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	cut it all or in pieces likewise the thickened part of it delicately, because if you do not cut it carefully, the water will return;
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac;	and if the testicle happens to be outside during your work, replace it when you have completed the work on the tunic;
puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then bring together the two edges of the testicle with a suture, then treat it like other wounds, until it is healed.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc;	And if you find the testicle corrupted by another disease, then you must tie the vessels that are suspensory, to prevent the flow of blood;
puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	then cut the testicle along with the suspensory ligament, and remove the testicle, and treat it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices;	And if fluid is collected in two parts together, know that these are two branches;
si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	then cut the other part as you did the first one equally, then wipe the blood, and put in the wound wool soaked in rose oil;
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	and above put other wool soaked in wine and oil, and place it on the two testicles, and put on top folded cloths, and tie it up with the bandage that is according to this form:
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil;	Then take two cloths, and fill them with carded wool according to this likeness, and let them be joined by stitching at the opening of the pants, and one of the ends should go over the buttocks up to the back, and the other to the penis area;
et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	and the other two ends over the two groins, and let all the bandage be gathered in the buckle of the pants;
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	and sometimes this ramification is treated with cautery instead of cutting with iron, and you should take a thin, knife-like cautery, and cut the skin of the testicles, and let it be heated as we have said, so that the white membrane that contains the water is exposed;
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	then take the cautery according to this form, and pierce this membrane with hooks, and peel it off with this thin, hot cautery:
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout;	And cut it in all the ways that you can, until you extract it all;
et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef;	and be careful that the fire does not touch the testicle;
et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve;	and know that this method is safer;
et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	and with less risk of bleeding, and better than surgery; 
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	and if anything gives you trouble, like a hot abscess or bleeding or something else, treat that which troubles you, according to what has been said before.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit;	And if the patient is afraid, and does not want to endure this procedure because of its dreadfulness, then perform a perforation, as I tell you, which is, when you are quite certain by the signs we have described that there is watery pus there, have the patient sit on a raised seat;
pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors;	then pierce the abscess in the lower part with the spatula wide open, and position the perforation lengthwise along the body;
et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer;	and let the opening be wide, so that all the liquid runs out freely;
puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee;	then put cotton on the area, and bind it, and leave it to drain the remaining liquid, then treat it until the wound is healed;
et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant;	and if the white cloth does not allow the liquid to flow from the opening of the wound, then you must insert a feather or the instrument used to draw liquid from dropsical patients, the form of which is shown above;
et eslarge I poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés VI mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	and widen the wound a little, and know that the liquid will return, and accumulate again after six months or around then, and when it has accumulated as before, the patient will continue this way throughout his life.
de l’aposteme des coions	Of the abscess of the testicles
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse;	Know that in the treatment of this branch (of medicine), there is fear in many situations, therefore it seems to me it is better to leave it alone;
et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	and I will tell you the procedure and the characteristics of the abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions;	I say then that many abscesses occur in the body, and particularly in the testicles;
et c’est par mout de cas.	and this is for many reasons.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion;	That is to say by an excess of sour and sharp (humor), which spreads to the testicles, or from a blow;
et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors;	and the color of the abscess is according to the color of the body;
et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief;	and there is no pain, and it is a serious abscess;
et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	and sometimes there is a severe, pale, and stony abscess, and of a weak color, and sometimes it comes from damage to an artery, or from swelling of a vein.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois;	When it is from damage to an artery, it is known by the disposition of a warm abscess, when you press it with your fingers;
et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	and you should not touch it.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars;	The one that is made from the swelling of a vein is known by its disposition to the pressure of the touch of the fingers, and one can well make the incision on this appearance, and on the other flesh;
et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	and you must cut the heart of the testicles, then stretch the egg upwards, and pull it away from the white membrane, and free the suspensory ligament from all parts of the egg.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope;	If the testicle is already adhered to this new flesh, then you must pull the testicle, and cut it;
et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	and if there is air in the tunica vaginalis, or in that which is inside the vessels, then you must free all this membrane, and cut it roundly.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the growth of the flesh is in the back part, then you must cut it all, and extract the testicle, as we have said.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when your work is completed, then fill the wound with wool moistened in rose oil and wine, then treat it with other treatments until it is healed.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess of the testicles
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait;	This is an abscess enveloped in a covering resembling a bud, with softening of the testicles, and the patient moves with difficulty when he walks;
et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	and the treatment of this illness is almost as dangerous as the one before, and yet we will tell you the procedure for it, according to what the ancients did.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment;	You must have the patient sit on a raised seat, then push the suspensory of the testicles down with your fingers, along with the vessels that are next to the penis, and have the assistant hold them, and stretch them firmly;
puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert, et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples;	then cut with a wide, transverse cutting spatula near the vessels, until they are exposed, and then dissect on each side, as we have described in the extraction of the arteries that are in the temples;
puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait I fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief;	then insert a needle with a double thread, and tie it at the first place where the screw came, and tie it again at the other end;
puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues;	then cut them in the middle straight, along the length of the body, and draw out the corrupted fluids;
puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions;	then treat the wound like the others where you generate pus, unless some vessel falls that nourishes one of the testicles;
car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz;	for no harm comes from this, and if a screw comes to all the vessels, then it is necessary to pull the testicles with all the vessels;
si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	so that the testicle does not lose its nourishment because of the incision of the vessels, and they dry up and cannot be helped.
de la routure dou syfac	of the rupture of the peritoneum/abdominal wall
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	The occurrence of this hernia is due to the tear that happens in the peritoneum/abdominal wall, or the stretching over the belly in the area of the groin, which causes the intestines to descend through this rupture to one of the testicles;
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes:	and this rupture is either of the peritoneum/abdominal wall itself, or from its stretching, and these two types arise from many causes:
ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	from a blow, or a jump, or shouting, or lifting a heavy load, and similar things;
et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	and the signs, when it is from the stretching of the peritoneum/abdominal wall, are that it occurs little by little, over a long time, and does not happen suddenly;
