Et s’elle ne revient par ceste cure, si pren une tauble de III bras de lonc, et chevé desoz la paroit, et li malaides soit en costé, et boute le chief de la tauble desoz la paroit, puis met le mileu de la tauble sus l’espinee;	And if it does not return by this treatment, then take a board three cubits long, and dig beneath the wall, and let the patient be on their side, and put the end of the board under the wall, then place the middle of the board on the spine;
et mette li mires ses piez sus l’autre chief de la tauble, et presse bien, tant qu’il reviegne au leu;	and let the physician place his feet on the other end of the board, and press firmly, until it returns to its place;
et se tu vues, si le fai au tornet qui torne a la main.	and if you wish, you can do this with a winch that is turned by hand.
Et est que tu fiches II tisons au chief dou malaide d’un bras de grant, et devers les piez II autres, et ait entre chescun tison, desoure et desoz, une paume d’espaice de lonc;	And you should place two firebrands at the patient's head, an arm's length away, and towards the feet two others, and there should be between each firebrand, above and below, a handspan of space in length;
et ait en chescun tison I pertus, ou li tornet corre, et soient li tison fermement en terre, si qu’il ne se muevent;	and each firebrand should have a hole through which the winch runs, and the firebrands should be firmly fixed in the ground so that they do not move;
et entre chescuns II tisons ait I tison tornant, sor coi li liien tornent, et ait en II tornans II petis tisons d’une paume de lonc, por torner le tornet;	and between each two firebrands there should be a turning bar, around which the ropes turn, and on the two turning bars, two small bars a handspan long, to turn the winch;
et puis lie lou lien qui est parmi les asseles au tornet devers le chief, et l’autre liien devers les piez a l’autre tornet, et chescuns des ministres torne son tornet a tout le liien, et li maistres mette l’espinee igal si com nos avons dit.	and then tie the rope that is through the armpits to the winch towards the head, and the other rope towards the feet to the other winch, and each of the assistants turns his winch with all the rope, and the physician places the spine straight as we have described.
Et quant elle est igalz, si met sus emplaustre desiccatif avec abun d’uef, et puis les estoupes, et puis l’estele d’une tablete de III dois de lonc, que porpreigne lou leu de la gilbositeit et la partie de l’espondile sainne, puis le lie d’un liien, si com nos avons dit, et use li malaides de norrissement subtil, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when it is straight, apply a desiccative plaster with plenty of egg, then the compresses, and then the splint of a small board three fingers long, so that it covers the place of the gibbosity and the healthy part of the vertebra, then tie it with a bandage, as we have said, and the patient should consume a light diet until he is healed;
et s’aucune chose vient en la fin de la santez, si covient aministrer medicines amollissans et asouajans, avec l’estele que nos avons dit ci devant;	and if any problem arises at the end of the healing process, it is necessary to administer softening and soothing medications, along with the splint that we mentioned previously;
et aucune fois i aministre on une piece de plonc, et aucune fois vient li apparance en la derriere spondile dou dos, et cuide on que ce soit dislocations;	and sometimes a piece of lead is applied there, and sometimes the appearance arises in the last vertebra of the back, and it is thought to be a dislocation;
et c’est li os qui apert, por coi on n’i doit mie avoir presumption:	and it is the bone that is showing, therefore one should not be presumptuous about it:
par aventure feroit venir la mort.	perhaps it would cause death.
des dislocations de la hainche	Dislocations of the hip
Saiches que as jointures de la hainche et as jointures de l’espaule ne vient fuers que dislocacions soulement, ne n’i vient mie si com as autres jointures;	Know that at the hip joints and at the shoulder joints only dislocations occur, not like in other joints;
et li jointure de la hainche est desaluee selonc IIII parties:	and the hip joint is dislocated in four ways:
dedens et defuer ,et devant et derrier;	inwards and outwards, and forwards and backwards;
et plus dedens c’aillors, et poc desalue devant et derrier.	and more inwards than elsewhere, and rarely dislocated forwards and backwards.
Et li conoissance de sa dislocations dedens si est que quant on joint la jambe malaide avec la sainne, si est plus longe, et apert plus li malaides genous que li sains, et ne puet li malaides doubler son genoil au feu;	And the sign of its inward dislocation is that when the injured leg is placed next to the healthy one, it is longer, and the patient's knee appears higher than the healthy one, and the patient cannot bend their knee to the buttocks;
et est li leus qui est delez enflez d’aposteme chaut, por ceu que li chiés de la cuixe vient lai.	and the area close by is swollen with a hot abscess, because the head of the femur comes there.
Et li signe de celui cui il vient au defuer, si est que cist accident sont contraire a ces devant.	And the sign of one that dislocates outwards is that these symptoms are opposite to the previous ones.
Et li signes de celui cui avient au devant, si est qu’il estent bien sa jambe selonc l’acomplissement;	And the sign of one that occurs forwards is that they can extend their leg fully;
toutevoie, ne double mie le genoil sens dolor, et s’on le vuet faire aler, si ne puet avant, et retient son urine, et enfle li angre, et quant il vait, si passe sus le talon.	however, they cannot bend the knee without pain, and if one wants to make them walk, they cannot move forward, and retain their urine, and the groin swells, and when they walk, they step on their heel.
Et li signes de celui cui il avient derrier, si est qu’il ne puet espandre son genoil, ne doubler, et est celle jambe plus torte de l’autre, et li angre est mollifié, et est li chiés de la cuixe au leu desoz les costes.	And the sign of the one that occurs backwards, is that they cannot extend or bend their knee, and that leg is more crooked than the other, and the groin is softened, and the head of the femur is positioned under the ribs.
Li ramenemens de ceste semblance de dislocation si est que tu rewarde se li dislocations est anciainne, et elle demore selonc sa disposition, si n’i a nule cure;	The reduction of this type of dislocation is such that you consider if the dislocation is old, and it remains fixed in its position, there is no cure;
et n’i covient mie qu’il ait presumption.	and there should be no attempt (to reduce it).
Et en celi dont li dislocation est fresche, et c’est des IIII manieres de dislocation, si te haste que tu tornes la jointe, et l’esten dedens et defuer, et la muef a destre et senestre;	And in the one where the dislocation is fresh, and it's one of the four types of dislocations, you must hurry to replace the joint, extending it inwards and outwards, and moving it right and left;
par aventure si revenra, et n’a mestier d’autre cure.	perhaps it will return (to its place), and no other treatment will be needed.
Et s’il ne revient en ceste maniere, si covient que tu apareilles I ministre fort, et esten la jambe fort a II mains, ou a I liien que soit liiez sus lou genoil;	And if it does not return in this way, then you must prepare a strong assistant, and extend the leg strongly with two hands, or with a strap that is tied above the knee;
et uns autres ministres estende sa main desus en teil maniere qu’il boute ses mains desoz ses asseles, puis l’estrigne d’un souef liien sus la cuixe;	and another assistant should extend his hand from above in such a way that he puts his hands under his armpits, then tightens it with a soft band above the thigh;
et uns autres tigne lou chief dou liien;	and another should hold the end of the strap;
et estendent amont et aval tuit a une fois, tant que li malaide soit levez de terre a une fois, et demoure pendans.	and they all extend, upwards and downwards, at the same time, until the patient is lifted off the ground at once, and remains hanging.
Ceste maniere d’estension si est commune as IIII semblances, et se li dislocation est revenue, si com nos avons dit, c’est bien.	This method of extension is common to the four types, and if the dislocation has returned, as we have said, it is good.
Se ceu non, si covient mettre cure a sa semblance.	If not, then a treatment appropriate to its type must be applied.
Quant li dislocations est au pardedens, si covient que tu sovines le malaide sus son costeit sain, puis met le liien sus la racine de la cuixe, et le leu qui est desoz l’angre, puis estent le liien en haut devers l’angre, et devers la forcele;	When the dislocation is inwards, you should lay the patient on his healthy side, then place the strap on the root of the thigh, and the place that is below the groin, then extend the strap upwards towards the groin, and towards the navel;
puis preigne uns autres ministres ses bras, et embraice le gros leu de la cuixe malaide, et l’estende au defuer forment:	then have another assistant take his arms, and embrace the thick part of the injured thigh, and extend it outwards strongly:
si revenra a son leu maintenant;	it will return to its place immediately;
et ceste maniere de dislocation est plus legiere des autres.	and this type of dislocation is easier than the others.
Et se tu ne la pues serrer en ceste maniere que nos avons dit, si covient que tu lies les II piés dou malaide ensamble d’un fort liien souef sus les II talons, et sus les II genous, et soit li jambe malaide estendue II dois plus que li autres;	And if you cannot fix it in this way that we have described, then you must tie the two feet of the patient together with a strong soft strap on both heels, and on both knees, and the injured leg should be extended two fingers more than the other;
puis soit pendus sus le chief d’un fust, et soit en sus de terre II bras de lonc;	then let him be hung by the top of a piece of wood, and be two arm-lengths above the ground;
puis comande a I ministre qu’il embraice le chief de la cuixe, et soit uns autres ministres pendans avec le malaide, qui embraice forment la cuixe, car li jointure revient maintenant hastanment.	then order an assistant to grasp the top of the thigh, and let another assistant hang with the patient, who firmly grasps the thigh, for the joint will return to its place quickly and suddenly.
Et quant li dislocations est au defuer, si gise li malaides, si com nos avons dit en celui qui a gilbositeit, et estraigne I liien sus la jambe malaide proprement, et sus le peis ausi;	And when the dislocation is in the nape of the neck, the patient should lie down as we have described for someone with gibbosity, and tighten a strap on the affected leg firmly, and on the weight as well;
puis met II tisons, I au chief et I autre as piez, puis fiche I tison entre les cuixes au malaide emmi la forme;	then place two firebrands, one at the head and the other at the feet, then insert a firebrand between the patient's thighs amidst the mold/support;
et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.	and have wet cloths placed around it, so that it doesn't injure the patient, then each assistant should stretch towards him, and the physician should set the dislocation evenly with his hand.
S’elle revient, c’est boin.	If it returns (to its place), that is good.
Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	If not, put (him) on a table, and press as we have described for gibbosity, and have the patient lie on their healthy side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit;	And when the dislocation is forward, one must extend the affected leg quickly, and according to what I have said;
et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	and the physician should put his effort on the diseased groin, then press with the other hand, and extend it downwards towards the knee.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches;	And if the dislocation is backwards, one should not extend the patient downwards, nor lift them off the ground, but rather they should be as if the hip were dislocated backwards, as we have said about lying on both hips;
et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table;	and (the patient) should be on their face, and the limb extended as we have said previously, and one should press on the joint against the table;
et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz;	and it will be correct when the patient extends their legs, and they are even;
adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve;	then bring the thighs together, and apply the plaster, and bind it with a bandage, so that the hip does not move;
et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus;	and (the patient) should rest for three or four days, then unbind it, and apply the plaster again;
et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors;	and if you see that they are even, bind it as before, and leave it for three days;
puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	then unbind it, and have him walk gently, until the limb is strengthened.
de la dislocation dou genoil	of the dislocation of the knee
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres:	The knee can be dislocated in three ways:
c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier;	namely, inwards and outwards, and backwards;
et ne desalue point devant.	and it does not dislocate forwards.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez;	And the sign is that you ask the patient to bend their leg at the thigh, and if it does not bend at the thigh, you know that it is dislocated;
et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez;	and the restoration of all of them is that you have the patient sit upright, and extend their leg if they can, and put your back against their face, and put their foot on your feet;
puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment;	then take their knee in your palms, and pull between your fingers, then bend both sides of the knee strongly;
et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement;	and another assistant extends their foot, until the knee returns to its place, and the sign is that they can bend their leg at the thigh easily;
et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie;	and apply the plaster, and bind the leg to the thigh, and tie them together tightly for three or four days, then untie it;
et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	and the patient should not exert themselves to walk, until the limb is strengthened.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	And if the limb is not aligned, then the assistant applies strong traction, as we have described in the treatment of the hip, until it is healed.
de la dislocation dou talon	of the dislocation of the heel
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The heel is sometimes sprained, and sometimes completely dislocated, both inwardly and outwardly.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee:	And the sign is that the ankle is swollen, and leans forward on the side where it is dislocated:
li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	The reduction is easy, and one should extend it gently with one's hands when it is only sprained.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville;	And when it is completely dislocated, you must have the patient sit upright, and an assistant hold him firmly by the leg, above the ankle;
puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut;	then pull the foot towards you with your right hand, and then with your left twice, then stretch it upwards, and gently push the foot upwards;
et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet;	and do this twice, as we have said, pushing and pulling the foot;
s’elle revient, c’est bien;	if it returns, that's good;
se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient;	if not, repeat the procedure, because it will return;
et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide;	and if it cannot return this way, have the patient lie on their back on the ground, and firmly fix a stake in the ground between their thighs, and tie cloths around it so that it does not injure the patient;
puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet;	then let the assistant hold the thigh, and another assistant extend the foot with their hands or a cord, that they tie above the ankle;
puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent;	then each assistant extends evenly, and the stake should always be between the patient's thighs to hold the patient steady when extending;
puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	then the physician evenly reduces the dislocation with their hands, and another assistant holds the healthy leg underneath, and the dislocation will return quickly.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois;	And when it is in place, apply the plaster and padding on top, and tighten firmly, and tie the foot to the leg, and watch the nerves that are on the ankle behind, so that the bandage is not too tight;
puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain;	then leave it for two or three days, and if the bandage loosens, tighten it;
puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors;	then untie it on the third or fourth day, and forbid the patient from walking for four days;
et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	and if he walks before that time, it is not certain that it will not dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if hot abscesses develop there, you must treat them as we have said elsewhere, until they are healed.
des dois	of the fingers
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When the fingers are dislocated, they must be gently extended without force, and this is an easy thing.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;	And if the dislocation is in any joint of the back of the foot, you must make the patient sit on a flat surface or on a table, completely upright, and place your foot on the part of the joint that sticks out, then press firmly with your foot, until it returns;
et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie;	and when it is even, and nothing sticks out, place a two-legged table under the sole of the foot, then bind it tightly, and leave it for three days, then untie it;
et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and let him rest until he is healed.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	of wound and dislocation together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	When a wound occurs with the dislocation, and one wants to treat it, it often happens that the patient dies:
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	so do not be presumptuous in the treatment, unless you are wise in the art and you have practiced it for a long time, and unless you are compassionate and merciful and careful, not reckless;
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	and at the beginning, use soothing things for a hot abscess, and leave the patient in God's hands, if you see no hope of health;
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	and when you see hope, then immediately return the limb to its place, before a hot abscess develops there;
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	and when the limb is in place, then administer things that soothe a hot abscess, and treat the wound, as appropriate, with drying ointments;
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	and if along with the dislocation there is a fracture, and small bone fragments separated, remove them, and do what we have said about simple maladies;
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	and beware of entering the path of fear, according to what I have said, for this benefits you according to your Creator, and for the safety of your soul and your body.
